1b1(rgyud): sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi brgyad bzhugs s+ho/
2a1(rgyud): sarba bud dus ma yol// garnams
2a2(rgyud): sa bgu nas ma
2a3(rgyud): bA ra nam/ ud ta ra tan tra/ bod skad du/ sangs rgyas rdza
2a4(rgyud): ma/ u dka1/ dgad du/ phyi
2a5(rgyud): cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba/ mkha' 'gro ma sgyu ma/ bde ba'i
2b1(rgyud): mchog ces bya ba'i rgyud phyim/ dpal rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo//
2b2(rgyud): sems dpa' sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ gas
2b3(rgyud): ba mchog gi dges pa na// thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs/ 'di ni rang
2b4(rgyud): 'byung bcom ldan 'das/ gcig tu rab tu che ba'i lha// sangs rgyas thams cad
3a1(rgyud): mnyam sbyor ba/ mkha' 'gro sgyum bde ba'i mchog/ chags med chag
3a2(rgyud): dang bral ba min// dbu mar yang ni mi dmigs so// bud med kun gyi rgyu ma'i rgya// 'di
3a3(rgyud): ni gnyis med theg pa'i mchog/ sgyu ma dag ni thams cad pas// bud med sgyu ma khyad
3a4(rgyud): par che// ngo bo nyid kyis mthu dag gis// rang bzhin gyis ni de grub pa'i// 'jig
3b1(rgyud): rten gsum 'dir bud med 'di// gus par byed pa dag tu 'gyur// brnyed dang bde dang dga' kun
3b2(rgyud): gyis// ngan pa spyod pa'ang 'grub par 'gyur// rang gi ngo bo yongs bsgyur nas// bud med kun gyis
3b3(rgyud): sgyum 'grub// ngo mtshar sgyu ma'i phyag rgya 'di// mkha' gro ma zhes brtag bstan te/ de ni na mkha' gro/
3b4(rgyud): bzhes// khams las mngon du brtags pa ste// nam mkha' kun du spyod 'grub pas// mkha'
3b5(rgyud): 'gro ma zhes rab tu grags// thams cad ma lus bde mchog gis// sangs rgyas thams cad
4a1(rgyud): mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro ma zhes rab du grags// de ni na mkha'agro ba zhes/ sangs/
4a2(rgyud): rgyas khams las rnam par brtags// kun du 'gro ba 'grub pa ni// sangs rgyas kun bdag mkha' 'gro
4a3(rgyud): ma'o// ma zhes bya ba bde bar bshad// sangs rgyas kun gyi bde chen yin// sgyu ma thams cad rab sbyor ba/
4a4(rgyud): mchog tu bde bas bde ba'i mchog/ kun tu kun nas thams cad ni// bdag nyid rtag tu thams cad kun/
4a5(rgyud): sangs rgyas la sogs rten g.yo kun// kun gyis dngos por bdag gyur to// sems dang sems dpa'i
4b1(rgyud): ting 'dzin kun// byang chub spyod pa sna tshogs nyid// de bzhin bdud dang bdud las rgyal// de ni byang chub sangs rgya
4b2(rgyud): yin// rdo rje rdo rje 'dzin nyid dang // de bzhin pad ma 'chung // nor bu nor bu 'dzin nyid dang // de dag gi yang
4b3(rgyud): rigs yin no// de nyid 'dod chags 'dod chags bral// 'dod pa dang ni grol ba'ang yin// dus gsum srid
4b4(rgyud): gsum mchog gsum dang // 'jig rten gsum dang khams gsum dang // rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i/
4b5(rgyud): gnas pa thams cad de nyid do// 'gro ba dag ni ma lus kun// thams cad du ni 'di 'gyur ro// de la sogs pa
4b6(rgyud): mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i// dngos
5a1(rgyud): ngomams cad de yin to// nam mkha' kun gyim pasan dpal// rdo rje sems dpa'
5a2(rgyud): bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog go// bskal pa
5a3(rgyud): bye ba grangs med par// sangs rgyas thams cad thob pa yi// phyag rgya'i cho ga gang dag gis// tshe 'di
5a4(rgyud): nyid kyis thob 'gyur ba// de ni bdag gis thob par bya// sangs rgyas kun bdag bde ba'i mchog
5a5(rgyud): bdag nyid shin tu bsgrub pa la// sangs rgyas kun bdag bde ba'i mchog/ rnal 'byor yang dag ma yin
5a6(rgyud): sems// lha la dmigs par byed pa dag/ rnal 'byor gzugs brnyan rang bzhin te// lugs ma
5b1(rgyud): la sogs rnal 'byor skye// yang dag mchog sems rnal 'byor pa// lha la dmigs par byed pa dag/ rang gi dam tshig
5b2(rgyud): bdag sbyor ba// mi 'gyur dam pa 'grub par 'gyur/ gzugs brnyan lugs ma la sogs las// rnal 'byor 'byung
5b3(rgyud): bar mi 'gyur gyi// byang chub sems la rab brtson na// de las rnal 'byor lhar 'gyuraro// byang chub sems ni rdo rje ste// sangs rgyas//
5b4(rgyud): kun gyi bdag nyid yin// de bas thams cad bdag sbyor bas// sangs rgyas thams cad thob par 'gyur/ bdag nyid sangs rgyas thams cad
5b5(rgyud): dang // dpa' bo thams cad bdag yin no// de bas bdag nyid lhar sbyor bas/ bdag nyid rab tu bsgrub par bya// de yis sangs rgyas thams cad
5b6(rgyud): dang // dpa' bo rnal 'byor thams cad dang / rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad ni/ tshe 'di nyid la 'grub par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems
5b7(rgyud): dpas de skad gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba// mkha'
6a1(rgyud): 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog las/ de kho na nyid snang ba dam pa'i yul la 'jug pa ye shes kyis phyag brtag pa ste dang po'o// 'di ni rnal 'phya
6a2(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas tham cad mnyam par sbyor/ mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' sbyor bas/
6a3(rgyud): dbab pa thams cad rab tu 'grub// sangs rgyas cad mnyam sbyor ba// rnal 'byor dbang phyug bde ba che// de bas bde ba nyid kyis ni// sangs rgyas bde
6a4(rgyud): ba kun 'thob pas// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// rnal 'byor dbang phyug bde chen po// 'di la khrus dang bsdam mi dgos// dka' thub
6a5(rgyud): dka' ba spad mi dgos// dka' thub sdom pa med pa dom// bde ba dang ni dga' bas 'grub// de las ji ltar 'dod sprod cing // kun za de bzhin
6a6(rgyud): thams cad spyod// spyod pa ci dga' 'dod par byed// g.yo ba dga' kyang ci dgar byed// langs pa dang ni 'dug pa dang // 'chag gam ji ltar gnas
6a7(rgyud): kyang rung // dgod dam rab tu smra yang rung // gang na ji ltar spyod kyang rung // dkyil 'khor du yang ma zhugs pa 'am// sgrib pa kun dang ldan yang rung // rad
6a8(rgyud): gi lhar ni bdag sbyar ba// bsod nams chung yang 'grub par 'gyur// de nyid rnal 'byor 'di yis ni// thams cad sgrub pa byed pa na// ngan zos ngan spyod tham
6b1(rgyud): cad kyis// nyes pa dag tu yong mi 'gyur// bskal pa bye bar mi thob pa// sangs rgyas dam pa thams cad de// phyag rgya'i cho ga gang dag gis// bsgrub na kun du thob 'gyur ba//
6b2(rgyud): bdag nyid sgrub par byed pa'i mchog/ de ni bdag nyid brtag par bya// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' bdag
6b3(rgyud): sbyor ba// cha lugs ji bzhin bsgyur ba yis// thams cad sna tshogs phyag rgya'i mchog// bsod nams chung yang 'grub par 'gyur// rgyud 'di sgrubs pa tsam gyis ni// sangs
6b4(rgyud): rgyas thams cad byin gyis brlob// shin tu byin gyis brlab na ni// sangs rgyas thams cad 'du bar 'gyur// sang rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam par 'gyur//
6b5(rgyud): sang rgyas kun dang mnyam pa'i phyir// sangs rgyas thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// gang gi ldan pa 'di mthong zhing // rna ba kun tu mchod byed na// de yi sangs rgyas tha~Md kyang // mthong zhing mchod
6b6(rgyud): pa byas par 'gyur// 'di dang sangs rgyas thams cad la// mthong ba dang ni rig pa yis// dkyil 'khor bdag tu zhugs pa// bden pa dag kyang mthong bar 'gyur// mthong ba dang ni reg
6b7(rgyud): pa dang // thos pa dang ni drang ba yis// sdig pa kun las rnam grol zhing // sangs rgyas dngos grub thams cad 'grub// 'di dang sangs rgyas thams cad la// rnal 'byor thams cad mnyam sbyor ba
6b8(rgyud): bud med dag kyang rnam grol zhing // sangs rgyas byang chub reg par 'gyur/ kun tu kun nas thams cad ni// bdag nyid rtag par thams cad du// sangs rgyas thams cad dngos
7a1(rgyud): sbyor grub par// de yis bdag nyid mthong bar 'gyur// 'di ni bdag nyid kun gnas pas// mchod pa'i sprin chen thams cad kyis/ bkod
7a2(rgyud): ba rab 'byam tshogs dag gis// de bzhin gshegs pa mchod pa mdzes// thams cad bdag nyid sbyor mchod dang // rdo rje sems dpa' mchog nyid ni// sangs rgyas kun
7a3(rgyud): gyi rang bzhin te// bde ba'i mchog 'grub par 'gyur// rnal 'byor thams cad nyer sbyor bas/ dpal ni gzhir gyur 'grub par 'gyur// rnal 'byor kun ni bcom
7a4(rgyud): ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// de yi nye bar sbyor ba ni// khams gsum ma lus thams cad do// rnal 'byor kun gyis longs spyod kyis/
7a5(rgyud): ji ltar bde bar bsnyen byed cing // rang gi lha yi rnal 'byor gyis// bdag nyid rab tu mchod par bya// rjes su sbyor bas mchod byed byed// rnal 'byor kun tu bde ba
7a6(rgyud): dag/ bdag nyid kun du myang byed na// shin tu sbyor bas 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid kyis// rang sa ye na bde ba 'dis// rdo rje sems dpa'
7a7(rgyud): dpal tshe dang // lang 'tsho nad med pa de mchog 'grub/ kun du kun nas thams cad du// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyul bde ba'i mchog
7b1(rgyud): rtag tu de ni 'grub par 'gyur// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpas de skad gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i
7b2(rgyud): mchog las// dpal rdo rje sems dpa' kun du sbyor ba'i brtag pa ste gnyis pa'o// // 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/
7b3(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor bas// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog dpal// rdo rje sems dpa'i rnal 'byor pa// dpal ldan rang gi de tshig ste// sangs rgyas thams cad
7b4(rgyud): mnyam sbyor ba'i// rnal 'byor dbang phyug bde chen dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' sbyor ba yi// mthu nyid kyis ni thams cad du// phyag rgya bde ba chen po kun// so sor rjes
7b5(rgyud): su rab 'grub 'gyur// dpal ldan rdo rje sems sbyor ba'i// mthu nyid kyis ni thams cad du// rnal 'byor bde ba mos pa kun// so sor rjes su rab 'grub 'gyur// dpal
7b6(rgyud): ldan rdo rje sems sbyor ba'i// mthu nyid kyis ni thams cad du// bde ba mos pa'i dbang phyug kun// so sor rjes su rab 'grub 'gyur// dpal ldan rdo rje sems sbyor ba'i/
7b7(rgyud): mthu nyid kyis ni thams cad du// namakha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i// bud med mchog rnams skye bar 'gyur// de yi dam tshig des 'byung ba// sdug pa dam tshig bdag
8a1(rgyud): @#rjes 'brang // shin tu sbyor dang sbyor chen po// thams cad bdag nyid dam tshig mchog/ gcig bzhin du ni cig spyod pa// lhan cig spyod
8a2(rgyud): ba rjes spyad sdug/ sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma mchog tu 'bar// thams cad dga' ba ma lus pa'i// phyag rgya thams cad bde ba che/
8a3(rgyud): rtag pa dam pa lha mo yi// rgyal mos mchod pa thams cad mchog/ dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' sbyor// thams cad lha mo 'dus pas ni// ma lus bskal pa bzang
8a4(rgyud): po kun// bde bar so sor rjes su 'grub// phyag rgya 'di yis btab pa las// rdo rje sems dpa' che ba lha// na mkha'i dbyings kyis mtha' klas pa/ lha mo bde ba chen
8a5(rgyud): bo kun// thams cad rnal 'byor bde bas myong // sdig med stobs kyis ngo mthon du/ phan tshun du ni rab dga' bas// skyes bu'i tshul gyis dga' bar byed// dbang po
8a6(rgyud): kun las byung ba yi// mchod pa'i sprin chen thams cad kyi// bkod pa rab 'byam sna tshogs kyis// thams cad bdag nyid mchod byed byed// rnal 'byor bde ba thams cad kyi/
8a7(rgyud): dbang bskur bde chen las byung ba// rin chen sna tshogs thams cad kyis// rab tu spros pas dbang bskur 'gyur// lha mo kun gyi longs spyod la// ci bde bar ni bsnyen bya ba/
8b1(rgyud): bdag ni che ba'i lhar sbyor bas// bdag la bdag gis rab tu mchod// rnal 'byor thams cad bde ba yis// rjes su sbyor bas mchod byed cing // rtag tu myang bar byed pa na/
8b2(rgyud): shin tu sbyor bas rab 'grub 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad bdag nyid kyi// ra sa ya na'i bde des dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' che 'grub cing // lang tshe nad med bde mchog
8b3(rgyud): 'grub/ sangs rgyas kun gyi sku chen dang // sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung snyan pa// sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs che ba// sangs rgyas kun gyi mchod pa che// sangs rgyas kun gyi rgyal chen
8b4(rgyud): po// rdo rje 'dzin pa kun gyi bdag/ 'jig rten dbang phyug kun gyi gtso// rin chen dbang phyug kun gyi bdag/ de dag dang ni dga' spyod na// 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong lding // lha
8b5(rgyud): mo thams cad grub chen po// 'khor los bsgyur bar rab tu 'gyur// chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// na mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pas// dngos grub kun gyi bde
8b6(rgyud): bos pa// de las rgya che mchog gzhan med// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// rnal 'byor dbang phyug chen po des// 'di la tshe 'di nyid kyis ni// rnam pa kun tu mi
8b7(rgyud): 'grub pa'i// dngos grub kun gyi bde mos pa// chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// na mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas par// dbang phyug kun gyi bde mos pa// de las
9a1(rgyud): mnyam sgo cha chen gang yang med// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog des// 'di la tshe 'di nyid kyis ni// rnam pa kun du/
9a2(rgyud): mi 'grub med// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rjes sems dpas de skad gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam par sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro ma sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog
9a3(rgyud): las// lha mo thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje dam tshig gi brtag pa ste gsum pa'o// // 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje
9a4(rgyud): sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ lha mo kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// bskal pa bzang mchog
9a5(rgyud): 'dod pa ste// yang dag sbyor ba'i bde myong ba// 'dod chags ther zug brtan pa can// sangs rgyas kun gyi gzugs chen dang // dbyings dang dri dang ro dag dang // sangs
9a6(rgyud): rgyas kun gyi rig 'de la chog/ rang gi spyad par byud de/ sangs rgyas pa ma gyin grub pa// gzungs dang sa rnams de bzhin du// dga' bar spyod nas dang mi// bam
9a7(rgyud): bzang bud med ci nig smos// lha'i dngos grub dga' ba dang // sangs rgyas byang chub pa de chen po// bskal pa bzang ba bde byang bas// seM so rjes su rang 'grub 'gyur/
9b1(rgyud): dngos grub thams cad las byung ba// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi dpal// bskal pa bzang po longs spyod kun// rang gi spyod par de spyod do// rdo rje can gyi grub mchog dang //
9b2(rgyud): 'jig rten dbang po mchog gi dpal// sangs rgyas kun las bde dam pa// phrogs nas nye bar spyod par byed// khams gsum dag na ma lus pa'i// sangs rgyas rgyal srid
9b3(rgyud): chen po kun// rtsal gyi stobs kyis ngos 'thon du// phrogs nye bar spyod par byed// sangs rgyas kun gyi grub chen po// mchog gi dbang phyug dam pa dag/ kun nas phrogs
9b4(rgyud): te de spyod na// longs spyod gzhan lta smos ci dgos// mthu chen las ni bkra shis brtan// phrogs las grub dang dran las dga'// ngo 'thon stobs kyis phrogs nas kyang //
9b5(rgyud): de ni dad la sbyin par byed// ma lus 'jig rten gsum rgyal srid// 'jig rten dbang phyug kun dang bcas// ngo mthon stobs kyis phrogs nas kyang // de ni dad pas sbyin par
9b6(rgyud): byed// tshangs pa 'jug sel dbang chen gyi// mchog gi dbang phyug dam pa dag/ kun nas thogs te myur sbyin na// longs spyod gzhan lta ci zhig smos// de yis mi sbyin ci
9b7(rgyud): yang med// sangs rgyas don du bya ba kun// mi bya ba ni gang yang med// sbyin pa dang ni byed pa'ang yin// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yang // phrogs nas kyang ni sbyin byed
10a1(rgyud): na las mchog dag ni rab 'byab dang // dngos grub gzhan lta ci zhig smos// dngos grub mchog ni gdon mi za// sde rnams thams cad rab 'joms pa/
10a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi grub chen po/ 'khor los bsgyur bar rab 'grub pa// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgrum bde mchog gis// sangs rgyas kun gyi rdzu
10a3(rgyud): 'phrul te// rnam par 'brul pa rab tu 'jug/ la lar byang chub sems chen po// la lar spyod pa 'thun par 'gro/ la lar dga' ldan lha dag las// dam pa shin tu 'gro ba 'i//
10a4(rgyud): la lar skye ba rnam par dag/ la lar nges par 'byung ba gsal// la lar byang chub chen por gshegs// la lar bdud las rab tu rgyal// la lar byang chub mngon 'tshang rgya/
10a5(rgyud): la lar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor// la lar pha rol mu stegs rnams// chos dang 'thun par tshar bcad do// la lar 'jig rten gsum rgyal ba// grub pa kun gyi dbang phyug nyid//
10a6(rgyud): la lar rtog pa thams cad mchog/ grub dbang phyug bla na med// de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ sangs rgyas kun bdag bde mchog gi/ 'dul ba'i thabs su nges pa'i don/
10a7(rgyud): rnam par 'phrul pas dges shing rol// dngos grub chen po kun gyi mchog/ btan pa dbang phyug che ba'i bdag/ gzugs dang tshe dang kha dog stobs// dpal ldan do rje/
10b1(rgyud): sems dpa' bzhin/ 'gro ba bdag gis bsnyen bya zhing // de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis mchod// lha mo kun gyis dpal ldan mchog/ rdo rje sems dpar rab tu
10b2(rgyud): 'grub// sems can khams ni du ma dag/ ma lus par ni phyag rgyas 'debs// lha dang byang chub sems dga' dang // brtan par sems can rnams la sbyin// sangs rgyas
10b3(rgyud): kun bdag bde mchog gis/ sems can kun gyi don byed cing // ma lus lus pa med pa yi// bskal pa kun tu srid par gnas// bcom ldan 'das dpal rdo rje sems dpas
10b4(rgyud): de skad gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog las// sna tshogs thams cad kyi bskal pa bzang po mchog gi dngos
10b5(rgyud): grub ces bya ba// dpal dam tshig gi brtag pa ste bzhi pa'o// // 'di ni rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// sangs rgyas thams
10b6(rgyud): cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ yang dag bsgrub pa gcig pu nyid// ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du sbyar// rtog pa'i go cha thams cad la// grub pa
10b7(rgyud): dam pa mchog gi mchog/ sna tshogs las kyi sbyor ba yis// cho ga sna tshogs 'dod pa yis// sems can rnams ni 'dul ba dang // bde ba thams cad 'grub pa'i phyir/
11a1(rgyud): mnyam sbyor#bcom ldan rnal 'byor de nyid ni// sangs rgyas thams cad rnam 'phrul bas// sems can don kun rnam 'phrul na// myur du shin tu 'grub par
11a2(rgyud): 'gyur// nyin re 'am yang na zla re 'am// yang na de bzhin lo rer ni// ji bzhin byin gyis brlabs nas kyang // sangs rgyas bde mchog gang bya'o// khams kyi ngo bo thams cad
11a3(rgyud): dang // de bzhin srog dang rtsol las byung // rang gi lha yi cha lugs su// grub pa'i phyag rgyar rab tu bya// dkyil 'khor gang dang gang brten pa// sna tshogs phyag rgya'i mchod
11a4(rgyud): pa yis// slob ma'i tsho gas kun de dang der// mchod pa byas nas der sgrub po// de las gzhan yang rtog kun gyi// sangs rgyas thams cad rnam 'phrul pa// ci rigs par ni sprul
11a5(rgyud): byas pa'i// btam dag rab tu bshad par bya// sems dpa' sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos// rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ rtag tu da ltar byung ba bzhin// ngo bo nyid ni 'da' bar
11a6(rgyud): dka'// chog sa tshogs 'dod rnams la// las kyi sbyor ba sna tshogs kyi// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin la sogs// 'dul ba'i phyir ni byas pa yin// sangs rgyas la sogs brtan nam/
11a7(rgyud): kun// kun gyi dngos grub 'di 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ smra ba'i sbyor ba 'di yis ni// rnam pa sna tshogs kun gyi
11b1(rgyud): mchog/ sems ca kyi don mchog rnams// sangs rgyas la sogs 'dul bas 'grub// dpal rdo rje sems dpas dbugs byung ba'o// 'das pa'i dus na sngon byung ba//
11b2(rgyud): bdag nyid chen po rtag pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rabs la// 'gro ba'i tshul ni sngon byung ba// de tshe sems can thams cad ni// shin tu stong pa nyid la brtson// 'gron
11b3(rgyud): pa'i chos nyid la sbyor bas// 'gags shing yongs su mya ngan 'das// rnal 'byor de bzhin bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// grol ba thams cad rnam
11b4(rgyud): sbyang phyir// sangs rgyas sprul pa kun du bskyed// stong pa ma yin mi stong min// dbu mar yang ni mi dmigs te// shes rab pha rol phyin sbyor bas// thabs kyi snying rje bdag nyid rnams//
11b5(rgyud): de bas 'di ni snying rje'i thabs// shes rab pha rol phyin par gsal// rtog pa med pa'i chos rnams la// sems can don du yongs brtag pa// rnam par rtog la mos pas// zas
11b6(rgyud): cad rtogs pas brtag par bya// brag cha yi ni sgra 'dra ba// chos kyi tshig tu 'gyur te// de las theg pa chen po yi// yang dag yon tan rgyas pa'i glus// dus gsum pa yi dam tshig
11b7(rgyud): gsum// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bstod// mnyam nyid mi g.yo mnyam nyid mchog gi chos nyid can// thugs rje'i bdag nyid 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal sel bar mdzad// yon
12a1(rgyud): mam @#/ tan mtha' yas dngos grub thams cad sbyin mdzad pa// dri bad mi g.yo mnyam med dam pa'i mchog chos can// yon tan shin tu che ba'i cha lang tshad med do// dpe ni
12a2(rgyud): nam mkha' dang yang bskrun du yod ma yin// dngos grub mtha' yas mnyam med dpe dang bral ba rnams// sems can khams la dngos grub mchog rnams nges par brtsol// rtag tu/
12a3(rgyud): dri ma med pa thugs rje'i shugs las byung // smon lam grub pa med pa'i chos nyid cen// 'gro ba'i don grub rab tu brtson pa mtha' yas pa// thugs rje chen po'i bdag nyid rtag tu
12a4(rgyud): rnam par snang // tshad med tshad dang bral ba shin tu yongs rdzogs pa'i// bde bar gshegs pa'i go 'phang dam brnyes gyur kyang // khams gsum khams la dngos grub mchog rtsol
12a5(rgyud): mdzad pa yi// thugs rje'i spyod pa mi g.yo 'gag par yong mi 'gyur// e ma'o shin tu bzang po'i chos nyid mchog dang ldan// mchog sbyin rnams kyi nang na go 'phang mchog brnyes nas//
12a6(rgyud): khams gsum kun la rtag tu dngos grub mchog rtsol mdzad// mgon po des gsungs sgrib pa med par rab mkhyen par// dam tshig mchog gsum dngos grub dam pa bdag la rtsol/
12a7(rgyud): 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// yang dag yon tan rgya chen te// lan cig tsam ni brjod pas kyang // sangs rgyas thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun bdag nyid
12b1(rgyud): sbyor bas// bstod pa'i rgyal po 'di nyid kyis// dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad kyi// dam tshig gsum po 'grub par 'gyur// sku ni lta bas mi ngoms pa// thams cad bdag nyid bstan
12b2(rgyud): nas kyang / legs so zhes ni grub pa yis// mchog rnams kun ni rab sbyin mdzad// thams cad bdag nyid 'grub dka' dang // bsam thams cad yongs su rdzogs// sangs rgyas
12b3(rgyud): grub pa mchog kun dang // rnal 'byor dam pa'ang sbyin par mdzad// de nas de'i bsgrub pa dang // shin tu brtag pa'i dngos grub dang // gang gis srid pa 'di nyid la// dngos grub
12b4(rgyud): shin tu rtag thob bshad// rdo rje se gol tog pa yis// sangs rgyas thams cad bsdu bar bya// thal mo lan gsum rnam par gdab// dbang po gang dang gang lam gyur// de dag
12b5(rgyud): de yi ngo bor bya// shin tu mnyam bzhag sbyor ba yis// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor zhing // ji ltar dga' chos chags pa dang // sha da pa la sogs pa yis// ci nas yongs su
12b6(rgyud): mi skye bar// rtag tu tshad med bzlas par bya// kun tu kun nas thams cad ni// bdag nyid rtag tu rnam pa kun// sangs rgyas kun dang dngos grub pa// rab tu mthong zhing
12b7(rgyud): mchog grub bo// 'di yis sangs rgyas thams cad dang // de bzhin dpa' bo thams cad dang // de rje 'dzin pa thams cad du// tshe 'di nyid kyis 'grub bar 'gyur// sangs rgyan
13a1(rgyud): #/ kun gyi yon tan bsngags pa rgya che ba// bstod pa'i rgyal po mchog ni lan gcig grur blangs pa// kun du 'gro ba'i rnal 'byor brtag pa'i mchog/ dngos
13a2(rgyud): grub mi zad bde ba thob par 'gyur// bstod pa'i rgyal po 'di yis ni// thams cad bdag nyid dbang phyug mchog/ sna tshogs kun gyi rnam 'dul ba// de bzhin gshegs pa kun
13a3(rgyud): 'grub ste// de bas dam tshig gsum la sogs// rtog pa bla med thams cad kyis// na mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i// sems can khams ni rnam par grol// dpal rnam
13a4(rgyud): par snang mdzad kyis dbugs phyung ba'o// 'dus pa'i dus na sngon byung ba// bdag nyid chen po rtags pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rabs la// de tshe sems cad thos
13a5(rgyud): cad ni// shin tu khro gtum gdug par gyur// shin tu gdug cing khro ba yis// 'o dod 'bod pa ltung bar gyur// de nas 'phos nas sems can de// bag chags kyis ni 'tsham
13a6(rgyud): sbyor ba// shin tu gdug pa chen por gyur// blo ni bdud kyis byin brlabs nas// rims dang dug dang dbyig dug nang // phra men ma dang gnod byed gdon// bdud dang rnam par
13a7(rgyud): log 'dren nyid// shin tu gdug pa chen por gyur// gnas gsum po ni 'jig byed cing // bsgrub pa po ni rnams la'ang za// lha la sogs gang 'pho bar byed// bstan pa dag
13b1(rgyud): kyang 'jig par byed// de nas dbang por bcas pa'i lha// tshangs pa'i drung du nye bar dong // tshangs pa'ang lha dang dbang por bcas// 'jug sel la ni skyabacu dong // tshangs pa 'jug
13b2(rgyud): sel lha rnams kyang // lha chen drung du nye bar dong // tshangs pa 'jug sel dbang chen yang // rdo rje can la skyabasu dong // de nas bcom ldan rdo rje can// rdo rje sems dpa'i sbyor
13b3(rgyud): ba yis// rdo rje se gol phyag rgya ni// sangs rgyas thams cad bsdu bar mdzad// rdo rje sems dpa'i sbyor ba yis// dpung pa gnyis ni rdo rjer bcings// rdo rje se gol brdabs pa yis//
13b4(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad bsdu mdzad pa// de yi bka' tsam gyis bsgag nas// 'khor dang 'khor lo'i tshogs bcas pa// sangs rgyas thams cad gshegs gyur pa// gzhan
13b5(rgyud): lta smos ni ci zhig dgos// rdo rje se gol tog pa yis// 'jig rten gsum ni ma lus par// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin pa bcas// kun gyis til 'bru bzhin du rgyas// shin
13b6(rgyud): tu gdug pa'i gtum po la// zhi bas phan par mi 'gyur te// shes rab thabs kyi ngo bo yi// khro bor de bzhin gshegs kun mdzad// khro bor tshul can khros pas kyang //
13b7(rgyud): 'jig rten gsum ni bsreg byed na// sangs rgyas thams cad khros pa yis// khams gsum sa lus blam mi dgos// de bas sna yi rtse ba la// yid ni btan par yang dag 'thang/
14a1(rgyud): ra@#/ sna yi dbus ni dro ba las// rgyal bas phyag rgya'i sbyor ba phyung // bcom ldan de nyid rnal 'byor pa// rdo rje khro bor gyur nas byung // he ru ka dpal rdo rje che/
14a2(rgyud): 'bar bas thal bar rab tu 'jig/ sems can dpa' sngon po 'bar ba'i ngang // 'od kyi dkyil 'khor dbar po 'bar// 'jig pa chen po'i dus ltar drag/ dur khrod kyi
14a3(rgyud): ni me dang 'dra// 'bar ba chen po sgra 'bar ba// thod pa mang po'i dbu rgyan can// 'jig pa chen po'i dus ltar drag/ dur khrod bzhin du rab 'jigs pa// khro la sogs pa'i
14a4(rgyud): tshul ldan pa// zhal rnams sna tshogs 'gyur ba dang // smin ma khro gnyer bcas pas bsgyur// 'bar ba'i blta bas gar byas pas// gu lang dbang chen nye dang bcas//
14a5(rgyud): nyi zla gshin rje tshang bar bcas// gnas gsum dag ni 'bar byas nas// thal ba bzhin du rab tu 'jig/ rdo rje rdo rje kha T+wAM kha// dril bu'i sgra ni bsil ba yis// thams
14a6(rgyud): cad bab nas slar yang ni// thal bar gyur pa'ang 'tsho bar byed// de yi 'bar ba nyi ma las// byung ba'i grib ma mi bzad pa// bskyed nas ma lus 'dud la sogs// bdug
14a7(rgyud): pa rnams kyi khrag za nas// rgyal po de ni de dag dang // lhan cig dur khrod rnam par rol// thams cad rdo rje mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro'i dkyil 'khor bar ba yis/
14b1(rgyud): shin tu gdug cing khro drag pa'i// sems can khams ni rnam sbyangs nas// dag pa'i sangs rgyas zhing rnams su// sangs rgyas byang chub dag la bgod// rdo rje khro bo la sogs kyi//
14b2(rgyud): rtog pa bla med thams cad kyi// na mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa// sems can rnams ni rnam par sbyangs// dpal he ru kas dbugs dbyung ba'o// /
14b3(rgyud): 'das pa'i dus na sngon byung ba// bdag nyid chen po brtag pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rabs la// 'gro ba'i tshul ni sngon byung ba// de tshe sems can thams cad ni//

14b5(rgyud): pad mo chags par sbyor ba yi// rdo rje chos su gnas par gyur// ji ltar pad ma dmar po 'di// 'dam gyi nyes pas mi gos pa// de bzhin bag chags khams gsum gyi//
14b6(rgyud): nyes pa sna tshogs rnam par dag/ 'dis ni kun tu gzigs pas na// rgyal ba'ang dbang phyug nyid du 'gyur// dpal ldan spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang // rdo rje sems dpa' de

15a1(rgyud): ##/ spro// kun tu spyan ras gzigs dbang rgyal// pad ma gar gyis dbang phyug gyur// pad ma sgyu ma mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog des/

19a3(rgyud): tshig skyon med rtag la rol cig rol cig go// kye ma mchog tu gsang ba'i bdag po rang gi dam tshig ni// yin pa'i phyir na rab tu gsang ba'i lha mchog rnams so// 'gro ba'i rgyud ni rnams
19a4(rgyud): pa sna tshogs 'dul ba gsal bar mkhyen// dam tshig dngos po brtan g.yo kun gyi ngo bor gyur rgyal ba// kun gyi bdag nyid rnal 'byor bde ba mkha' 'gro sgyu ma'o// kye ma dam pa
19a5(rgyud): brtag pa'i dngos grub chen po rab bsgrubs ston// dzaHhUM baM hoHe ma ho/ bde mchog bde bas drang du gsol// rnam par sprul cing rnam par mdzad// a la la ho// de bzhin

19b1(rgyud): pa med par snang // rnam pa mang po'i 'dod chags rgyud kyi sems// ma lus lus pa med par 'dul mkhas pa// sgyu ma bde mchog de bzhin gshegs kun gyi// sgyu mas thams cad rab
19b2(rgyud): sbrul rnam par 'phrul// te na te te hUM// rnam pa mang po'i dga' ba'i rgyud kyi sems// ma lus lus pa med par 'dul mkhas pa// sgyu ma bde mchog de bzhin gshegs kun gyi// sgyu ma
19b3(rgyud): thams cad rab sprul rnam par sprul// hUM hUM hUM// rnam pa mang po'i khro bo'i rgyud kyi sems// ma lus lus pa med par 'dul mkhas pa// sgyu ma bde mchog de bzhin gshegs kun
19b4(rgyud): gyi// sgyu mas thams cad rab sbrul rnam par sprul// ru lu ru lu hUM b+h+yo hUM// rnam pa mang po'i srog gi rgyud kyi sems// ma lus lus pa med par 'dul mkhas pa// sgyu ma bde mchog/
19b5(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs kun gyi// sgyu mas thams cad rab sprul rnam par sprul// hUM shiSh+ya bi sha hUM// de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// na mkha'i
19b6(rgyud): dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i// rang byung rnams kyi glu yi rgya// nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpal// rdo rje sems dpa' la ni gnas// grub pa'i dbang phyug rab grub pas// thas cad
19b7(rgyud): bdag nyid 'grub par 'gyur// glu 'di dag ni blangs pa dang // lha mo kun gyis rab bskul nas// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid 'grub// dbang po
20a1(rgyud): ma @#/ kun las byung ba yi// mchod pa'i sprin chen rnam bkod pa// rab 'byam tshogs rnams thams cad kyis// kun gyi bdag nyid mchod par byed// sangs rgyas
20a2(rgyud): thams cad mi 'am sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyum bde mchog gis// dngos grub kun gyi bdag nyid ni// ma lus lus pa med par 'grub// ston pa'i phyag rgya bab pa yi// bud med dag
20a3(rgyud): kyang bsgrubs nas ni// rdo rjer bcas pa'i mtshan mar 'dzin// rnal 'byor mar ni rab tu 'gyur// de dag rang gi lha rnams dang // 'dra bar byin gyis brlabs bsgrubs nas// sngon
20a4(rgyud): med rol mo sil snyan gar// rnam par sprul pas 'grub par 'gyur// lha'i gzugs dang sgra dang dri// ro dang reg pa bde mos pa// bdag nyid rang gi ltar mthong zhing // mchod pa
20a5(rgyud): dag kyang byed par 'gyur// lha yi mchod pa mnyam sbyor ba// bskal bzang mchog gi 'dod chags can// rnam pa kun tu bskal bzang po// bde ba yang dag bsgrub par byed//

20a7(rgyud): dpar sbyor ba yis// mthu nyid kyis ni thams cad du// sna tshogs kun gyi bskal bzang po// rang gi bde ba nyid grub po// sangs rgyas kun gyi gzungs chen dang /
20b1(rgyud): dbyangs dang dri dang ro bde bas// rdo rje sems dpa' bdag nyid kyis// de yis rab mthong mchod pa byed// mchod pa thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// bskal bzang mchog gi 'dod/
20b2(rgyud): chags can// sangs rgyas thams cad bdag nyid kyi// dngos grub ma lus lus med 'grub// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde mchog gi// sangs
20b3(rgyud): rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid gar// de nas yang dag rang gsang bas// bud med dag ni bzhi rnams dang // gar gyi phyag rgya mchod pa yis// mchod pa thams cad dbul bar bya// /

20b7(rgyud): bar ma gyur dang // mchod pa dag ni mi 'byor pa// phyag rgya 'di yis mchod byas na/ mchod pa thams cad myur du 'grub// mchod pa'i sbyor ba 'di dag dang /
21a1(rgyud): mtho#lha mo bzhi po dag gis ni// me tog la sogs mchod byas nas// slob ma thams cad bzung bar bya// dngos grub 'dod pas

21a4(rgyud): rin chen dbang bskur bas// ji lta bar ni dbang bskur ro// dmar chen po dang ga bur bcas// tsan dan dmar po sbyar ba rnams// tshogs kyi dbus su bzhag pa la/
21a5(rgyud): g.yon pa mtshan 'dzin rdo rjer bcas// rang gi mtshan ni rnal 'byor ldan// srin lag dag ni mthe bo'i rtses// zhi ba'i btung ba bzhin myangs na// rtag pa'i dngos grub thob

21a7(rgyud): gna' ni bgegs byas nas// sangs rgyas thams cad mthun pa yis// mchog tu rtag pa'i bka' stsal pa// dam tshig sdom pa sbyin par bya// sangs rgyas thams cad
21b1(rgyud): mnyam sbyar ba'i// sdom pa nyams par khyed byed pa// ji snyed sangs rgyas thams cad dang // byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje 'dzin// lha dag dang ni mi rnams dang // de bzhin

22a1(rgyud): @yang dag rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dang // rdo rje can gyis bka' stsal to// rnal 'byor bcas dang gsang bcas pa'i/

22a3(rgyud): phyag rgya'i ye shes rjes bzung bas// rnam par snang mdzad mchog bzhin du// sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag nyid 'grub// de nas ro dang zas dang gnas/
22a4(rgyud): glu dang sil snyan la sogs pa// de dag mgon po rnams la dbul// rdo rje bla ma chen po dang // bdag dang gzhan la 'dod dgus mchod// de nas bdag

22a6(rgyud): dpa' dpal gyi tshul// rtog pa thams cad rab 'grub cing // rtog pa kun la rab sbyor ba'i// ngo bo nyid phyir chen po'i mchog/ sna tshogs las kyi sbyor ba dang /
22a7(rgyud): 'dul ba'i bdag nyid sna tshogs pas// sems can rnams ni 'dul ba'i phyir// de las gzhan pa'i tshul du bstan// rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin
22b1(rgyud): gshegs// thar pa thams cad rnam sbyang phyir// grol ba'i mkha' 'gro 'byung bar 'gyur// rang gi lha dang 'dra ba yin// rang gis byin brlabs bsgrub pa'i rgya// phyag rgya ji bzhin rjes 'thun
22b2(rgyud): pa'i// sangs rgyas sprul pa bsgrub par bya// gzhan yang rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// dam tshig la sdang rnam sbyang phyir// thams cad rnal 'byor dbang phyug mchog/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro 'byung bar 'gyur/
22b3(rgyud): gzhan yang shin tu rnal 'byor pa// ma lus pad mo rnam sbyang phyir// bskal bzang dam pa mi 'gyur ba// pad ma sgyu ma 'byung bar 'gyur// gzhan yang rnal 'byor bcom ldan 'das// nor gyi mchog ni rnam spyad
22b4(rgyud): phyir// nam mkha' kun gyi bdag po che// rdo rje nyi ma dpal 'byung 'gyur// rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das// drag shul sbyor ba sbyang ba'i phyir// rta 'grin pha rol rab gnon pa// rta mchog rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur//

22b6(rgyud): thams cad mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro sgyu me bde mchog 'grub// kun du kun nas thams cad ni// sangs rgyas 'phrul pa thams cad kyis// bdag nyid rtag tu
22b7(rgyud): rnam pa kun// kun gyi dngos por de 'gyur ro// kun tu sangs rgyas thams cad ni// sangs rgyas rnam 'phrul thams cad kyis// bdag nyid rnam pa 'phrul pa ston//
22b8(rgyud): lha mo kun dang 'dus pa yis// sangs rgyas sprul pa grub par byed// sangs rgyas sprul pa sgyu ma yis// sangs rgyas rnams kyi mdzad pa ston// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba'i//
23a1(rgyud): mapa' 'ab rgyas ga byed pas// 'angs gsus da/ ni sasus par/ dngas po dkun tu 'gyur ra/ 'angs skyes nas 'phrul pas/ sas rgyam do rje 'dzin pa mas

24a1(rgyud): mnyam sbyo@#pa sna tshogs dang / de bzhin chu bo'i 'gram dag gam/ rgyal khams gzhan las grub pa ru/ rdo rje rta ni bsgrub par bya/ cha lugs rnam pa sna tshogs dang /

24b1(rgyud): bar 'gyur/ kun tu sna tshogs bskal bzang po/ kun tu sna tshogs 'kho la can/ kun tu sna tshogs 'grub pa'i phyir/ dkyil 'khor kun tu sna tshogs pa'o// dkyil 'khor

25a1(rgyud): @ma @#spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang / log par lha dang ldan pas na/ bskal ngan mu stegs 'jig rten pa// dam pa'i nor mchog bsdud pa'i
25a2(rgyud): phyir/ bskal bzang rdo rje nyi ma dpal/ bdag gi bu la'ang ma chags pas/ bskal ngan dka' thub spyod pa kun// rgyal srid mchog rnams kun bsdus pas//
25a3(rgyud): mchog dpal ni bskal bzang // bdag med yongs su 'dzin med pas/ thub pa thams cad bskal pa ngan/ bde ba thams cad bdag bsgrub phyir/ kun gyi srob
25a4(rgyud): dpon bskal pa bzang // ltas ngan dam tshig la sdang ba'i/ slob ma thams cad bskal ba ngan// gsang ba'i don de yang dag nyid/ 'dir ni gsal bar shes pa yis//

25a6(rgyud): pa'i slob ma la/ gsang ba yang dag mtha' yas mchog/ thog ma nyid du gsal brjod pa/ kye khyod ci la dga' zhes dri/ bskal pa bzang la bdag dga' zhes/ 'jug pa pos
25a7(rgyud): kyang smra bar bya/ gsang ba'i yan lag 'di shes na/ ji ltar 'dod pa rab tu bzhug/ gsang ba yang dag mi shes na// g.yas pa yis ni bzhug par bya/ de ltar dkyil 'khor du
25b1(rgyud): zhugs nas/ de bzhin du ni yon phul te// gsang ba'i cho ga nyid ces pas/ mi 'gyur ba'i mchog 'grub bo// kun tu sna tshogs bla ma la/ yon mchog dag ni dbul bar nges/
25b2(rgyud): gang la yongs su btang dka' gang / de ni mchog tu bshad pa yin/ gang gi sdug pa'i mchog/ yang na shin tu khyad par can/ de dang de ni bla ma la/ de nyid mi zad 'dod/
25b3(rgyud): pas dbul/ yang na de nyid 'dod 'gyur ba 'am/ 'on te sems la dgos pa dag/ de sbyin yang na dgos par bya/ de ni chung yang mchog yin no/ de ni gal te mchog bdog
25b4(rgyud): la/ de yang ngan pa'i yon phul na/ kun gyi slob dben brnyes pas na/ de nyid rtag tu sdug bsngal thob/ bu mo shin tu brgyan pa 'am/ de bzhin chung ma sdug pa dag/ phul
25b5(rgyud): nas rin gyis zla ba ni/ sangs rgyas byang chub mchog gi yin/ mi chen bdag gis phul nas su// slar yang rin gyis zla ba ni/ rdo rje 'dzin dpal sbyor ba yin/ yon de mtsho/
25b6(rgyud): gi yon yin no// mu tig bzang dang nor bu dang / shin tu dkar ba'i ras zu ba dang / de bzhin rta ni dkar po dag kapad mo can gyi yon mchog yin/ rgyal srid longs spyod gter rnams dang /
25b7(rgyud): gos mchog rgyan gyi tshogs rnams dang / de bzhin mchod pa thams cad ni/ rdo rje nyi ma'i yon yin no// shin tu brtan pa'i rta dag dang / glang po shin tu brgyan pa dang // shing rta rin chen
26a1(rgyud): ba #gang ba dang // rta'i rgyal po'i yon yin no// khams kyi rang bzhin thams cad dang / srog dang rtsa'i de bzhin te/ sangs rgyas rin chen dbang bskur ba
26a2(rgyud): mkhas pa rnams pa sna tshogs brtag/ skye bo dang ni dpral ba dang / ldan pa gnyis dang lhag pa ru/ sangs rgyas rin chen thams cad kyi/ dbu rgyan mi 'gyur dab pa'o// khams kyi
26a3(rgyud): rang bzhin thams cad dam/ srog dang rtsa yi de bzhin te/ thod pa rin chen dbu rgyan nam/ sangs rgyas gtsug gi nor bu dag/ kun tu sna tshogs bla mar ni/ kun gyi slob dpon
26a4(rgyud): kun la bya/ rgyal srid thams cad rnam dag la/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ rin chen ngo mtshar gcig las byas// de bzhin sna tshogs rgyan gyis sbas/ sangs rgyas pad mos
26a5(rgyud): dbang bskur bas// sleb ma thams cad dbang bskur ro// sangs rgyas rin chen rdo rje phyed// rdo rje'i rigs la rdo rje yin// spyan ras gzigs kyi de rje ska/ nor bu 'dzin gyi nor bu yin/
26a6(rgyud): sangs rgyas rin chen pad mo dang // rdo rje ner bu de bzhin du/ thams cad mchog ni ta mchog dpal/ rang gi dbang bskur bsdus pa'o// blugs ma 'am ni byas pa'am// brdungs pa
26a7(rgyud): 'am ni bris kyang rung / sna tshogs rab tu legs pa yi/ mtshan ma'i phyag rgya rab tu btag/ kun tu sna tshogs bskal bzang po/ rang byung rnams kyi mtshan ma'i rtsa/ nam mkha'i
26b1(rgyud): dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i/ lha mo rnams kyi bde ba mchog/ gzhu dang mnga' dang de bzhin du/ bskal babang de ni bskal pa bzang / yod pa dang ni kha T+Te khA/ rdo rje h+ya gram de
26b2(rgyud): bzhin no/ pad me rgya gram dpag med tshe/ sangs rgyas kun gyi tshe bsgrubs pa/ lha mo'i tshogs rnams thams cad kyi/ mtshan ma'i phyag rgya tshegs bsgrub bzhin// mda' dang
26b3(rgyud): de bzhin tshangs pa'i mgo/ de bzhin 'khor lo'i phyag rgya dang / rdo rje tri shul phyag rgya'i mtshan/ dpag bsam shing dang lcug ma dang / pad mo ta 'grin 'phang mtho ba// !
26b4(rgyud): mgrin ljang khu de bzhin no// phag gi mche ba grub pa dang // zla ba nyi ma de bzhin no// rin chen sna tshogs snod chen du/ sangs rgyas gzugs kyi ra sa yan// thams cad
26b5(rgyud): bdag nyid myong bskal bzang / mtshan ma'i phyag rgya sna tshogs bzhag/ gling bu dang ni bi wang kun/ mu kun ta dang mu ra dza/ me tog bdug pa mar me dang // sna tshogs
26b6(rgyud): dri rnams de bzhin no// de la sogs te mtha' yas mchog chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i// mtshan ma'i phyag rgya dam pa'i
26b7(rgyud): tshogs/ nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na dpal/ rdo rje sems dpa' nyid la gnas// grub pa'i dbang phyug rab zab pas/ thams cad bdag nyid grub par 'gyur/ chos
27a1(rgyud): mtha byar@#gos dang ni lhung bzed dang / de bzhin du ni khar sil dang / dam pa'i chos kyi glegs pas dang / mtshan ma'i phyag rgya'i tshogs bzhan no// de bzhin lce'i phyag rgya dang /
27a2(rgyud): cha lang dang ni rnga dag dang // rdo rje dang ni rin chen snod/ mtshan ma'i phyag rgya sogs gzhan no// de bzhin sangs rgyas gzugs brnyan dang / me long dang ni rnga yab dang // rdo rje ser dang 'phrin
27a3(rgyud): las bcas// de bzhin mig gi phyag rgya dang / rdo rje 'bar dang kha T+wAM ka/ thod pa kham phor de bzhin no// dmar chen dang ni snying chen dang / sha chen po 'ang de bzhin te/ rnon po mda' dang
27a4(rgyud): de bzhin 'dren// chang dang chu yang de bzhin te/ lcug ma rlung gis bskyod pa dang // ras dang de bzhin me dag ni/ rdo rje khro bo'i rgyal po'i dpal/ bdug pa thams cad za ba yi/ mtshan mI
27a5(rgyud): phyag rgya grub pa'i tshogs/ rnal 'byor dngos grub rab bsgrub pa'o// pad ma sna tshogs dmar po dang / ljang khu de bzhin dkar po dang / 'thing ka ser po le ba gan dag/ pad
27a6(rgyud): ma'i mtshan mchog rnam pa bdun/ pad ma sbrang po bud med brgya/ de bzhin chos kyi 'khor lo dang / gsal zhing dpal bskyed rdo rje dag/ pad mo mtshan ma'i tshogs gzhan no// gzhu
27a7(rgyud): dang mda' dang ral gri dang / de bzhin du ni 'bar ba'i me/ dbang bskur gter dang rgyal mtshan dag/ mchod pa'i mtshan mas bsdus pa'o// de bzhin sna tshogs pad mo dang
27b1(rgyud): do rgya gram de bzhin te/ mtshan ma'i phyag rgya 'grub pa gnyis// rgyal srid thams cad 'joms pa ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad la sogs pas/ dngos po bstan g.yo ma lus kun// rang
27b2(rgyud): byang rnams kyi mtshan ma'i rgya/ na mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'o// de skad bcom ldan de bzhin gshegs/ rdo rje sems dpa' dpal gyis gsungs/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang maH
27b3(rgyud): par sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro ma sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog las/ dkyil 'khor gyi phyag rgya shes pa'i brtag pa ste// / bdun pa'o// de nas gzhan
27b4(rgyud): yang bshad pa ni/ rdo rje sems dpa' dpal gyi lha/ rnam pa kun tu sna tshogs mchog/ mchod pa thams cad rnam sprul pa'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis dag gis// 'jug
27b5(rgyud): mo mthe'u chung mdzes par bsgyur/ dpal ldan g.yon pa 'gying ba'i thabs/ g.yas pa ba dan gsum par bya/ srid zhur bcas pa steg pa'i mchog/ bdag nyid rdo rje sem
27b6(rgyud): dpa' dpal// 'dzum dang bcas pa'i mig gis blta// bsam pa g.yos pa'i phyag bya'o// sangs rgyas rdo rje pad mo 'dzin/ rdo rje nyi ma khams gsum pas/ skad cig gis
27b7(rgyud): kyang phyag byed na/ khengs pa gzhan lta ci zhig smos/ drag po dbang po nye dbang bcas/ nyi zla gshin rje tshangs par bcas/ du btud de rab tu phyag 'tshal nas/ las
28a1(rgyud): mnyam sbyor #rnam thams cad byed par 'gyur/ rdo rje dpal gyis thal mo bsgrub/ bsam pa g.yon pas phyag byas pa'i/ sangs rgyas mchod pa legs byas na/ ma lus lus
28a2(rgyud): pa med par 'grub/ smin ma g.yon pa 'degs tshul gyis// ru lu ru lur bcas dgod na/ tshangs pa nye dbang drag por bcas/ khams gsum pa rnams phyag byed 'gyur/ thal mo pad ma
28a3(rgyud): kha 'bus bzhin/ rang nyid sbyor ldan snying khar bcing / mthe bo mthe chung 'dab ma bzhin/ rgyas btud pa yi phyag kyang bya// lus kyi yan lag thams cad ni/ sa la bsnyal te phyag bya ba/
28a4(rgyud): snying kha dang / ni spyi gtsug tu/ thal mo sbyar te phyag bya'o// dpal ldan rdo rje 'gying ba'i thabs// 'dzum pa'i mig gis phyag byas nas/ khams gsum pa yang phyag byed na// mthus snyems
28a5(rgyud): gzhan lta ci zhig dgos// phyag 'tshal phyag rgya shes pa'o/ gar gyi rgyud rnams ji snyed pa/ de bzhin bya ba'i tshul ston kun/ de dag rdo rje sems dpa'i rgya/ rang gi don rnams 'grub byed
28a6(rgyud): ba// 'gying dang bcas pa'i tshul byas nas/ ji ltar tshul bzhin gar byed cing // bskor ba'i gar rnams sna tshogs kyis// mchod pa sna tshogs dbul bar bya/ lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis
28a7(rgyud): dag gi/ 'dzub mo ba chung mdzes par 'gyur/ g.yon pa'i 'dzub mo khu tshur bcangs/ g.yas bapa dan gsum par bya/ phyag rgya 'di las btab na naM/ sangs rgyas kun dang 'grogs
28b1(rgyud): ba dang // dngos grub chen po mchog kun gyi/ dbang phyug chen po 'grub par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang 'grogs pa/ dpal bskal ba bzang po zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// snyems 'dzin
28b2(rgyud): chen por bcas pa yi// sbyor bas de ni btegs nas su/ 'gram pa'i phyogs su longs bsgyur nas/ spyi bo'i 'tshams su bzhag par bya// thams cad 'bebs pa'i gar byed pas// gar byas
28b3(rgyud): de nas phab nas su/ bskal bzang hUM zhes bya ba'i glus/ mchod pa thams cad dbul bar bya/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba/ dpal bskal pa bzang po zhes bya ba'i
28b4(rgyud): phyag rgya'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis dag gis/ 'dzub mo mthe gnyis mdzes bsgyur ba'i/ rdo rje phal mo sbyar nas su// de bzhin g.yon du bsgyur bar bya'o// de na sbor bas bteg nas ni
28b5(rgyud): bskal bzang oM zhes bya ba'i glus/ mchod pa thams cad dbul bar bya// dpal rdo rje thal mo bsgyur ba sangs rgyas kyi mchod pa'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis dag gis/ 'dzub mo mthe
28b6(rgyud): chung mdzes bsgyur te/ rdo rje phal mo gyen du dgrol/ mchod pa'i gtor ma kun gyi tshul/ dur khrod cha lug gar byed pas/ phyag rgya 'di yis gar byed cing / bskal bzang rdo rje drag por 'ged
28b7(rgyud): mchod pa thams cad dbul bar bya/ dpal rdo rje he ru ka'i bal mo ste mchod pa'i gtor ma thams cad kyi cho ga'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis dag gis// 'dzub mo ma'i chung mdzes
29a1(rgyud): panyam sbyor@#bsgyur te/ g.yas g.yon thal mo brdabs pa yis/ mchod pa thams cad dbul bar bya/ dpal pad ma gar gyi dbang phyug gis bal mo'o// lag pa g.yas g.yon gnyis
29a2(rgyud): dag gis/ 'dzub mo mthe chung mdzes bsgyur te/ rdo rje rin chen thal sbar nas/ mchod pa thams cad dbul byar bya/ re ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dpal rdo rje rin chen zhes
29a3(rgyud): bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// gyen du mthor zhing thur du 'bebs/ bskor zhing de bzhin sgrub pa dang / me tog bdug pa mar me mchog/ dri yi mchod pa 'byung ba'o// gang ba 'am 'on te stong
29a4(rgyud): ba 'ang rung // yang na ci 'byor pa yis yang // dam tshig nyams bsgrubs pa yis// mchod pa thams cad 'grub par 'gyur/ phyag rgya 'di rnams bcings nas/ ni// sangs rgyas thams cad
29a5(rgyud): mchod par 'gyur/ dngos grub dbang phyug grub pas kyang / kun gyi bdag nyid mchod par 'gyur/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i// rang

29a7(rgyud): dbang phyug bde chen dang // dngos grub las dang bde ba dag/ 'di yis mi 'grub gang yang med/ mchod pa rab 'byam grub pa rnams/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub// Da ces dpal
29b1(rgyud): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas gsungs so// sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba/ mkha' gro ma sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog las// mchod pa thams cad dang mnyam
29b2(rgyud): bar sbyor ba/ dpal bskal pa bzang po'i dam tshig gi rtog pa ste/ brkyang ba'o// de nas gzhan yang bshad pa ni/ rdo rje sems dpa' dpal
29b3(rgyud): gyi lha/ kun tu sna tshogs mchog rnams kyi/ phyag rgya thams cad rnam sprul pa'o// sems dpa' sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos/ rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ gsang ba'i mchog
29b4(rgyud): ni dges pa na/ thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs/ bde ba kun la zhen pa dang / dngos grub thams cad rnam dag phyir/ rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ zla ba nya ltar gtsang
29b5(rgyud): ma'i sku/ 'dod chags kun la chags pa'i phyir/ chags pa chen po bcom ldan 'das/ rdo rje sems dpa'i phyag rgya 'ang / dmar po sna tshogs 'byung ba'i 'od/ khams gsum dag
29b6(rgyud): ba rin chen gzhan/ sangs rgyas rin chen lta bu med/ sangs rgyas kun gyi rin chen che/ dbu rgyan can ni de bas mchog/ gzhan gyi nor min ma thogs pa/ lha'i chu yis dag bste/
29b7(rgyud): mthu dang zab nyid dag dang / rang bzhin gyis ni grub pa'o// yod pa'i phreng ba'i dbu rgyan dang / sangs kyim gtsug gi nor bu can/ kun nas nyon mongs 'jig rten dbang /
30a1(rgyud): sa @#/ mi 'jed la sogs de grub pa'o// rdo rje sems dpa' dpas sbyor ba/ lha mo kun dang 'dus pa yis/ kun tu sna tshogs bskal bzang ba/ mkha'agro ma ni thams
30a2(rgyud): cad 'grub/ sangs rgyas rdo rje pad mo 'dzin/ rdo rje nyi ma khams gsum pa/ rgyas btab rmongs byas bsrang nas ni/ las rnams kun la sbyor bar byed/ phyag rgya 'di yis btab nas ni/
30a3(rgyud): 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong lding / lha mo kun mchog dpal dang ldan/ rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'grub/ mchog tu dga' ba la rab tu sbyor ba bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje sems dpa'
30a4(rgyud): bde ba'i mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// g.yas dang g.yon pa'i sbyor ba yi/ bde ba'i cha lugs gar byed cing / sems dpa'i dkyil mo dkrung bcas/ nas/ dpung rnams
30a5(rgyud): thams cad rab tu 'joms/ dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i dkyil mo dkrung ngo // zla ba'i kha dog 'dzum pa'i nas/ dngos grub thams cad dag pa dang / pad ma'i 'dod chags rnam dag
30a6(rgyud): phyir/ brla'i dbus ni dmar la dkar/ phyag mchog lo ma sngon po 'dra/ de bzhin bde ba'i dbang phyug dang / bde bar reg pa'i dbang phyug pas/ dkar zhing ser ba'i brla dang
30a7(rgyud): ldan/ lha rjes sna tshogs kha dog mchog/ 'bar ba sna tshogs 'khrug pa'i 'od/ pad ma sna tshogs la gnas pa/ thams cad dag par rab tu gnas// sangs rgyas pad mo la so
30b1(rgyud): mchog/ rin chen sna tshogs gis brgyan dang / sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa yis/ mi 'jed la sogs brgya byin bzhin/ bya ba dang ni bzlog pa dang / 'phrog pa dag kyang lhan/
30b2(rgyud): bar mdzad/ bdag la 'khrud pa'i phyag rgya yis/ yan lag thams cad phrogs par 'gyu ba// phyag rgya 'di yis btab na ni/ 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong lding // dpal ldan 'dod
30b3(rgyud): ba kun la dbang / rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'grub/ mchog tu dga' la rab tu sbyor ba bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje bde ba'i mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rnam pa sna tshogs
30b4(rgyud): dam tshig chags/ bde ba 'bar ba'i gar byed pas/ bdag la 'khyud pa'i phyag rgya mchog/ dbus kyi lha mchog chen po ni/ phyag rgya 'di yis rnal 'byor pa/ 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro
30b5(rgyud): 'ong lding / bde chen dbang phyug dpal dang ldan/ rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'grub/ mchog tu dga' ba rab tu sbyor ba bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i dam tshig bde ba'i
30b6(rgyud): mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// ser la kha yi chul dag tu// de grib T+wAM ga bzung ste/ bdag la 'khyung ba'i phyag rgya ni/ bad bzas rdo rje hra gram mchog/ phyag rgya 'di yis
30b7(rgyud): btab na ni/ 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro'ang rdzing / dpal ldan tshe dang gzhon grub pa/ rdo rje sems dpa' rab tu 'grub/ mchog tu dga' ba la sbyor ba/ bskal pa babang po dbas da
31a1(rgyud): nas 'byor bde ba'i mtshag sa pazhes bya ba'i rtsag ca'o// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas khal por grub/ bdags 'byung ba'i byag rgya mas/ nga
31a2(rgyud): dpa' dpal sbyor ba/ dbus kyi lha mchog rin po'o// phyag rgya 'di yis rnal 'byor pa/ 'dod pa bzhin du 'gro 'ong lding / dpal ldan tshe dang gzhon grub pa/ rdo rje sems dpa' rab
31a3(rgyud): tu 'grub// mchog tu dga' ba rab tu sbyor ba bskal pa bzang po dpal bde ba'i mchog rol pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi
31a4(rgyud): mnyam pa// na mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i/ rang byung phyag rgya sna tshogs rnams/ na mkha'i kun gyi skabs na dpal/ rdo rje sems dpa' la gnas te/ grub pa'i dbang phyug
31a5(rgyud): rab bsgrubs pas/ thams cad bdag nyid 'bar bar 'gyur// sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par spor ba/ mkha' gro ma sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog gi rtsa ba'i phyag rgya'i tshogs so// gtsug
31a6(rgyud): lag ji ltar rjes mthun pa/ dpal rdzogs rgya chen gar dag gis/ mda' bzhi yongs su 'bangs pa ni// bdud bzhi dag las rgyal bar 'gyur/ tshangs pa chen po'i mgo dpal rdo rje
31a7(rgyud): mnga' zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rkang pa gteg cing rab pa dang / bshibs te mchongs pa'i stobs dag gis/ 'khor lo byas byas ston na ni/ khams gsum dag las mchongs par
31b1(rgyud): 'gyur/ dpal rdo rje mthu bo che zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// bya ba dang ni bzlog pa dang / phrogs pa dag ni khyad par du/ sna tshogs khyad par gar byed cing / khams gsum dag ni bsdu bar
31b2(rgyud): bya// dpal rdo rje gar gyi dbang phyug ces bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// lcagasam gang yang rung bzung nas/ bdag la 'khyud pa'i phyag rgya yis/ bud med thams cad brtsed na ni/ dpag bsam
31b3(rgyud): shing dag rab tu 'grub/ dpal rdo rje 'dod pa'i lha mo zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// myang ba brtul bltar byas pas/ drag po dbang po nye dbang bcas/ nyi zla gshin je tshangs pa yi/ 'jig
31b4(rgyud): rten gsum dag skams par byed/ dpal rdo rje rta gdong zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// sna'i myang ba'i dub pa yis/ drag po dbang po cag nye dbang bcas/ nyi zla gshin rje tshangs pa yi/
31b5(rgyud): khams gsum yang ni bdud par byed/ dpal rdo rje phag mo zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o/ mig tshugs zhen pa blta ba yis/ drag po dbang po nye dbang bcas/ nyi zla gshin rje tshangs pa yi//

31b7(rgyud): tshangs par bcas/ thal bar gyur pa 'ang 'tsho bar byed/ dpal rdo rje kun gyi bdag nyid khams gsum thar 'tsho ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// / gling bu len pa'i chu/
32a1(rgyud): ma na@#ston cing // ji sa babs pa'i kar byed pas/ mangs pakyi dbang drag por bcas/ 'gro ba gsum dag dbang du byed/ dpal rdo rje gling bu'i dbang shes
32a2(rgyud): ba'i phyag rgya'o// pi wang len pa'i tshul ston cing / ji ltar bcas pa'i gar byed pas/ las rnams grub pa rab 'byam dang / dngos grub ma lus myur du 'grub/ dpal rdo rje bi
32a3(rgyud): wang bde bas rmongs par byed pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// / cang te tshul ston rnal 'byor pa/ ji ltar babs pa'i gar byed pas/ rims dang gdon dang dug zhen pa'i/ sdug bsngal
32a4(rgyud): thams cad myur du sel/ dpal rdo rje cang te'u sdug bsngal thams cad sel ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rdza nga'i tshul ston rnal 'byor pa/ ji ltar babs pa'i gar byed pas/ gnas gsuM
32a5(rgyud): dag ni ma lus pa/ ska cig tsam gyis 'bebs par byed/ dpal rdo rje rnga rnga'i myos par byed pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// phyag rgya gar gyi mchod pa yis/ mchod pa thams cad byas
32a6(rgyud): nas ni/ rang byung gar gyis mchod pa rnams/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ rims dang dug dang dbyig dug byed/ phra men gdon gyi gnod pa rnams/ skor ba'i gar rnam
32a7(rgyud): sna tshogs kyis/ skad cig pam gyis ni bar 'gyur/ drag po dbang po 'i dbang bcas/ ti tha gshin rje tshogs bcas pas/ byas btab ma byas thos pa yang / gcig tsam gyis 'a/
32b1(rgyud): bar byed/ de la sogs pa'i mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa/ namakha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa'i/ rang byung lha mo'i phyag rgya rnams// nam mkha' kun gyi skabs na
32b2(rgyud): dpal/ rdo rje sems dpa' la gnas te/ dngos grub dbang phyug rab grub pas/ thams cad bdag nyid 'babs par 'gyur/ sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba/ mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde
32b3(rgyud): mchog gi/ rab tu 'grub pa'i glu rnams kyis/ bla na med pa'i dngos grub thob/ de nas phyag rgya'i ye shes 'di/ dpal ldan rdo rje mchog gi glu/ las rnams thams cad rab bsgrub cing /
32b4(rgyud): srid pa shin tu bsgrub pa ni/ rdo rje sems dpa' bde chen skal bzang dpal tshogs bdag las bsgrubs la rtogs par mdzad du gsol// kye de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi bde ba mkha'
32b5(rgyud): 'gro sgyu ma sna tshogs bde ba'i mchog gis ni/ 'gro ba'i rgyud rnams rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul mchog 'grub pa bdag la grub par mdzad du gsol// a la la ho/ de bzhin gshegs
32b6(rgyud): ba'i sna tshogs gar rnams bstan du gsol/ dza hU~M baM ho/ kye bde ba mchog gi bde bas zung cig rnam par sprul pa hUM gis snang bar mdzad du gsom// a la la ho/ de bzhin/
32b7(rgyud): gshegs kun sna tshogs mtha' 'gro sgyums slob ma bzung du gsol/ sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba/ mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ kun tu nas thams cad ni//
33a1(rgyud): sa rgya 'di nyid kyil ni byung du 'grub/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang mthas par sbyor ba mtha' 'gro sgyu ma'i rnal 'byor gyi phyag rgya shes pa'o// rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das
33a2(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ thar pa thams cad rnam dag phyir/ sangs rgyas phyag rgya dpal gyi gnas/ don dam rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ gtse ma gser gyi kha dog bzhin// chag
33a3(rgyud): med la sogs chags chen phyir/ dkar zhing sna tshogs gsal ba'i mdangs/ chos kyi rgyal srid rab bsgrub pa/ rin chen chos las lhag pa med/ de bas theg chen byang chub
33a4(rgyud): sems/ rgyal ba rdo rje rin chen can// g.yas pa'i mthe bo gung mo gnyis/ g.yon pa'i khu tshur bcings pa yis/ ma sar kun la reg pa ni/ rtsa ba'i phyag rgya min par grags/
33a5(rgyud): 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ shes rab pa rol byin gsam yin/ byang chub sems ni bskyed pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ste/ phyag rgya 'di yis btab na ni/
33a6(rgyud): sa pa ma phyin pa ma' tsas kyis sa pa// grags par 'gyur badzin/ byang chub sa ni babyang pa dang / kyi 'bas na/
33a7(rgyud): khartse sangs rgyas nyid du rig par bya/ mchog tu rtag pa'i sangs byas sa/ gang gis ldan pa 'di mthong zhing / rnam pa kun tu mchod byed pa/ de mis sangs rgyas rtag pa'i mcho//
33b1(rgyud): mthong zhing mchod pa byed par 'gyur/ sems ni bskyed ma thag tu yang / chos kyi 'khor lo legs par bskor/ dpal dam tshig ces bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// g.yas pa'i yan lag
33b2(rgyud): gnon pa yis/ g.yon pa'i yan lag kun las rgyal/ nga sems dpa'i dkyil mo dkrung bcas nas/ bdud rnams thams cad rab tu 'joms/ dpal rdo rje dkyil mo
33b3(rgyud): dkrung ngo // rdo rje khu tshur bcas nas su/ lag pa g.yon la bkab na ni/ sangs rgyas kun blo dngos grub rnams/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ de bzhin dpal ldan he ru
33b4(rgyud): ka'i// rdo rje khu tshur che dga' ba/ dpa' bo glad pa'i dngos grub rnams/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ pad mo'i bud med khu tshur ni/ de bzhin g.yon pas bkab na
33b5(rgyud): yang / byang chub spong pa rab 'grub rnams/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ rin chen 'dzin pa'i khu tshur yang / lag pa g.yon pa bkab na ni/ sangs rgyas nor gyi dngos
33b6(rgyud): grub rnams/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ sangs byas khu tshur bcas nas su/ lag pa g.yon pas bkab na ni// sangs rgyas kun gyi tshe 'grub pa/ ma lus lus pa
33b7(rgyud): med par 'grub/ bud med phyag rgya bcings nas su/ lag pa g.yon pa bkab na ni/ dngos grub thams cad byar 'grub pa/ ma lus lus me bar 'grub/ rta mchog dpal gyi
34a1(rgyud): mamathong #/ khu tshur kyang / lag pa g.yon pas bkab na ni/ thams cad 'gugs par rab 'grub pa/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ dpal grub spyan gyi grwa/
34a2(rgyud): tshur yang / lag pa g.yon pas bkab na ni/ snang ba thams cad rab grub pa/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub/ dngo po sangs rgyas kun slob pa/ gnyis pa de bzhin dpa' bo
34a3(rgyud): yin// gsum pa kun tu bzang mo'o// bzhi pa mi zad snod yin no// sangs rgyas yang dag kun dpal ldan/ de bzhin zhal bzangs gzungs ma yin/ sprin chen mo ni bdun
34a4(rgyud): ba ste/ brgyad pa na mkha' spyan yin no// gzungs thams cad kyi phyag brgya'o// phyag rgya shes pa 'di dag gi/ sangs rgyas sprul pa'i glu mchog ni/ 'grub par 'gyur ba med
34a5(rgyud): ba'i mchog/ las rnams thams cad rab bsgrub pa/ slong bar byed pa brtan bsgrubs pa/ de bzhin sna tshogs rgyas pa dag/ sha rdzi'i dbyings kyi glu blangs nas// d+he ba ta yi
34a6(rgyud): glu blangs so// 'jig rten khams mang rdul phran grangs snyed khyab par 'bros pa yis/ rgyal ba'i don rnams rab tu phra ba'i rdul gyi grongs snyed pa/ sbrum pa'i sku rnams rab
34a7(rgyud): tu phra ba'i rdul gyi grangs snyed ni/ srid pa bde chen de bzhin gshegs kun rnam 'phrul sna tshogs kyis/ rdul phran grangs snyed de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par sprul pa mdzod//
34a8(rgyud): ho dpas rnam par snang mdzad sbyor ba la/ a la la to/ de ring grub par mdzad/ glu 'di dag ni blangs pa yis/ nam mkha' thams cad mnyam sbyor ba/ mkha' gro sgra
34b1(rgyud): ma gdon mi ga// des na bud med pani rnams dang / rang gi yang dag gsang ba yis/ cho ga rgyas pa'i tshul bzhin du/ me tog la sogs mchod par sh+ya/ de bzhin gshegs
34b2(rgyud): ba'i phyag gya shes pa'o// rnal 'byor de nyid bcom ldan 'das/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ dam tshig la sdang rnam sbyang phyir/ dur khrod dpas kyi phyag byar
34b3(rgyud): gnas/ shin tu gdug cing gtam pa la/ zhi bas phan par mi 'gyur te/ shes rab thabs kyi rnal 'byor gyi/ rnal 'byor bde mchog dam par 'gyur/
34b4(rgyud): sangs rgyas khros byung khro bo ni/ thal bar 'jig pa mchog yin te/ sems dpa' sngon po 'bar ba can/ 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor dbar por snang // gzhan gyis/
34b5(rgyud): ma yin mi phrogs pa/ lha rdzas chu yis dag pa ste/ de bzhin nyid dag dang / mthu dang ngo bo nyid kyis 'grub/ gos chen po dang klubs pa che/ sha chen po dang sbrang ci che
34b6(rgyud): dur khrod kun gyi 'byung po yi/ phyag rgya dbang ldan dbang phyug mchog shin tu khro gdug gtum po yi// sems can khams mang nam sbyang phyir/ 'di ni dpal ldan
34b7(rgyud): he ru ka'i/ rdo rje rgya chen dbang phyug mchog zad pa'i 'phreng ba'i rabu can can sangs rgyas gtsug gi nor bu dag rgyal sring thams cad rab 'grub pa/ ma lus dus
34b8(rgyud): pa mad par 'grug/ de rel ni ri rjes bcas/ dris bus dkris pa'i grwa bcas pa/ dpas ldan te ru ka babs pa'i/ phyag rtsa ma tshogs nas 'phrul par/
35a1(rgyud): mnyaM spyo/ #sangs rgyas rdo rje pad mo 'dzin/ rdo rje nyi ma khams gsum pa/ rgyas btab rmongs byas de zos nas// thal bar gyur na'ang 'tsho bar byed/ dpal/
35a2(rgyud): ldan rdo rje he ru ka rdo rje bab pa rnam par 'phrul ba pad ma gar gyi dbang phyug zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// se ral kha yi tshul dag tu / kha T+wAM kha la rgyab rten byas/ lag pa
35a3(rgyud): g.yon pa thod pa thogs// g.yas pa ba dan gsum par bya/ nam mkha'i phyag rgya'i rnal 'byor pa/ nam mkha' kun tu 'gro bar bya// bud med la sogs rin
35a4(rgyud): chen mchog/ dngos po thams cad mkha' las 'byin/ phyag rgya 'di yis yongs btab nas/ bde bar lhags pa'i tshul ston pas// namakha' la ni kun blags te//
35a5(rgyud): bdag gi sbyar ba de spyad do// drag po dbang po nye dbang bcas/ nyi zla mkha' gro mi bzad bcas/ mkha' las sgyu ma kun blangs nas/ lus pa med par de
35a6(rgyud): za'o// nam mkha' thams cad mnyam par sbyor ba bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma'i mchog ces bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// / g.yas dang g.yon pa'i sbyor
35a7(rgyud): yis/ bde bar 'bar ba'i gar byed pas/ dkyil mo dkrung ni byed bcas la/ rkang ba rang gi brdas mnan na/ drag po dbang po nyi dbang bcas/ tha
35a8(rgyud): gashrIn rje tshangs bcas pa/ rgyas btab rmongs byas bslangs nas su/ gar dag byed cing des za'o// de nyid kyis ni sbyor ba yis/ de nas bde bar
35b1(rgyud): brla bsdams pas/ legs par bsdams te phyir btags nas/ rab tu bkram te btang bar bya// sgyu ma de dag nyid kyis ni/ de dag brla brag bskyed
35b2(rgyud): pa yis/ bskal bzang lha dang mi rnams kyi/ bud med kun la de bskyed do// bde bar reg par mnyam par sbyor ba/ bskal pa bzang po dpal rdo rje drag po
35b3(rgyud): gnas pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// de nas gzhan yang rab bshad pa/ sangs rgyas mkha' yi dkyil 'khor du/ dpal ldan he ru 'bar ba yi// phyag rgya sna tshogs
35b4(rgyud): gnas pa'o// zhi ba drag po rmongs pa'i mchog/ dga' ba'i gar byed 'gyur bar bcas/ shi ba lnga pa pa'i sbyor ba yis/ bde ba'i phyag rgya rab tu gnas
35b5(rgyud): zhi ba drag po rmongs byed dang / gyen du dbugs 'byin gar byed lus// lta ba'i phyag rgya dgos grub mchog gsang ba'i sbyor ba bde mchog gi me tog bdug pa sbyor
35b6(rgyud): ba'i mchog/ chang dang chu dang lcug ma dang / ras dang me tog grub pa yis// khyad par du ni rgyas 'debs so// rtse gcig mnyam par sbyor ba yis/ sbyor ba'i gnyer
35b7(rgyud): ba bde ba sbyin/ mngon par gtong zhing se gol rdo ba/ dal bus gyen du dbugs 'byin pas/ g.yon du lta zhing lag pas drang / 'o byed 'khyud pa de bzhin te/ gar byed/
35b8(rgyud): rab tu rmongs pa dang / zas dang gsang ba'i lus rnams dang / tshangs pa chen po'i mgodang ni/ de bzhin 'jig rten gsum las rgyal/ de bzhin palab 'dren pa dang /
36a1(rgyud): mnyam sbyor/ @#rang gi phyag rgya'i tshul ston dang / dur khrod dag gi gar byed dang / de bzhin rlung gi dkyil 'khor dang / rab tu 'jigs pa sreg pa'i me
36a2(rgyud): las kyi phyag rgyar rab tu gnas// dang por rgyas 'debs ma yi n+ya/ snying 'dren ma'i gnyis pa'o// gsum pa shin tu rmongs byed ma'o// de bzhin bzhi pa 'deg byed ma yi/
36a3(rgyud): lnga pa gar byed ma'i h+ya/ drug pa gsod ma'i yin par bshad/ bdun pa za ba mo'i n+ya/ brgyad pa las kyi phyag rgya yin/ de nas phyag rgya 'di kun gyi// phyag rgya'i las
36a4(rgyud): rnams bla na med/ phyag rgya'i bdag nyid kun 'joms pa/ khyad par du ni bshad par bya/ dpal ldan rdo rje dbang mo slong // gar dag byed cing byas na ni/ rgyas btab rmod/

46a6(rgyud): tshogs la de yi tshegs kyi zas/ yon dang bcas par dbul bar bya// mchod pa'i sbyor ba 'di dag gis/ sdig pa kun las thar bar 'gyur// bsod
46a7(rgyud): nams thams cad 'phel bar 'gyur// de bzhin rtag par bsrung bar 'gyur// rims dang dag dang dbyig dag dang // mkha' 'gros rtse dang gdon rnams
46a8(rgyud): dang // bdud dang sems can dmyal ba rnams// 'di yis rab tu zhi bar 'gyur// dngos gru ba rnams dang phun sum tshogs// dga' dang de bzhin
46b1(rgyud): ba dag po dang / sangs rgyas dam pa thams cad dang / phyag rgya'i mchog rnams grub par 'gyur/ gar gyi phyag rgya shes pa'o// rab tu dga' ba rjes
46b2(rgyud): su chags pa'i dga' ba'i mda' gzhu rab tu phra ba'i rgyas btab pas/ rab tu dga' bar sbyor ba'i bde bas myos pa bde ba thams cad bdag la grub pa
46b3(rgyud): mdzod/ rab tu ba de mchog rnam pa sna tshogs rnam par rgyal mtshan bsgreng ba'i longs sprod dang / rab tu dga' ba'i dbang phyug che mchog sgrub pa de bzhin gshegs
46b4(rgyud): pa bzhugs he rta mchog ho// rab tu sna tshogs bde ba'i mchog la rol cig ho/ bde bas rab slong rnam par rol hUM snang bar mdzod/ a la la he/ de bzhin
46b5(rgyud): gshegs pa kun gyi mkha' 'gro sgyu ma sna tshogs kyis/ slob ma bzung du gsol// kye bde ba'i mchog grub par mdzod/ e ma ho bde ba bde ba rtsol//
46b6(rgyud): dam pa rab tu zhags par mdzod/ bdag la rab tu dges par 'gyur/ a la la ho/ e ma'o shi shi zhags shig mkha' 'gro bde ba'i mchog/ yongs su
46b7(rgyud): bskor nas kun tu zhugs// glu ni 'di dag blangs pa yis// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba/ mkha' 'gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ grub par 'gyur ba
46b8(rgyud): gdon mig/ ngo rje sems dpa' snang ba dang / rdo rje rin chen bla na med/ de rje chos ni gsung ba dang / ngo rje las ni byed par 'gyur/ hUM de je las kyi mngar gsu
47a1(rgyud): mnyam s+ho/ #phyag 'tshal lo// dpal rdo rje chags pa'i dam tshig la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje kha TaM kha rab tu 'jigs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// dpal rdo rje dri/
47a2(rgyud): bu 'khrol ba la phyag 'tshal lo// la lar rab tu drag cing skye bo drag la drag po'i bud med sku ltar rab tu snang / 'gro ba mtha' yas gdul phyir la lar rab tu rno ba'i
47a3(rgyud): 'khor lo phyag na bsnams pa'i sku// la lar rab tu des shing zhi ba mi 'gyur sbyin pa tshangs pa'i sku yang ston par mdzad/ la lar rab tu 'bar ba'i chags pa bad/
47a4(rgyud): ma'i rgyal po dam tshig bdag la grub par mdzod/ thams cad dbang skur dbang phyug dam pa mi zad gter mchog bdag la grub par mdzad du gsol/ kun mchog
47a5(rgyud): rgyal mtshan rnam rgyal bsgreng ba rdo rje rin chen shin tu che ba bdag la mdzod/ la lar mkhas pa'i bzugs kyang 'dzin/ la lar dus mtha'i dus ltar drag ga la lar
47a6(rgyud): rgyal ba'i dbang po bzhin du ni/ la lar rta mchog 'dod sbyor 'dod pa bsgrub/ rdo rje'i glu'i mchod pa'i phyag bya shes pa'o// me tog dkar dang dmar ba dang / 'thing
47a7(rgyud): kha ser po kun bsdus na/ me tog phyag rgya mchog 'di ni/ 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga la spro/ rgya skyegs 'bring kha ljang gu'i mchog chen sna bzhi yis bcos pa dang /
47a8(rgyud): dkar po lnga'i phyag rgya dag/ snga ma bzhin du mnyam par 'grub/ khams las byung ba thams cad dang / sog dang rtsa ba de bzhin du/ rnam par mdzes shing
47b1(rgyud): dri zhim pa/ snga ma bzhin du mnyam par 'grub/ tsan dan gnyis dang bla rtsi dang / ga bur na ga sha la gi/ bdug pa bu ram dang sbar ba/ las rnams thams cad
47b2(rgyud): rab bsgrub pa'o// gan dang dri dang gu gul dang / sa rdza ga bur bla rtsi dang / rdzas 'di dag las bcos pa'i mar/ me mar byas na snang ba skyes/ tsan dan gur gum
47b3(rgyud): spri ka dang / ga bur dang ni bla rtsi dag/ btsos pa'i bdug pa 'grub pa ste/ spos kyi phyag rgya spos mchog 'gyur// ka ko la dang sug spel dang / bla sgang ga bur
47b4(rgyud): bla rtsi dang / 'di rnams zhib mor btags pa ni/ seng ldeng bu ram dag dang sbar// shing rtsa pa ta pe ta dang / na le sham dang ga bur sbar// ha las ka ri'i shing mar
47b5(rgyud): gyis/ spras pa li ni spos yin no// dpal rdo rje sems dpa'i phyag rgya sbyor ba/ me tog dmar po sangs rgyas la/ rdo rje can la sna tshogs pa/ 'jig rten dbang

47b7(rgyud): rdo rje nyi ma la/ mar me 'phreng ba sangs rgyas la/ rdo rje can la mar me bdun/ spyan ras gzigs la mar me brgyad/ steng ni rdo rje nyi ma la/ sangs rgyas
47b8(rgyud): rnams la tsan dan spos/ rdo rje can la gur gum yin/ spyan ras gzigs pa can dbar / gapur rdo rje nyi ma la/ me tog kun dang bdug pa kun/ de bzhin
48a1(rgyud): mangs snong bya mar semams cad dang / sras rnamasathams cad de rje nyal dbul du rung / mchod pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya shes pa'o// sgeg po

49a8(rgyud): gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rdo rje thal mo mnyam sbyar te/ lan gnyis nor bu rin chen du/ ji ltar rigs par mnyam byas nas/ 'dzub mo mche
49b1(rgyud): bong rtse mo bzhin/ yongs su bsgyur te gtogs nas su/ dpral bar legs par bzhag nas ni/ khams gsum bdag po rgyal ba dag/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub

52a1(rgyud): mnyam sgyu#slob ma'i dkyil 'khor btsud nas kyang / sngon gyi mchog dag blangs nas ni/ rdo rje ming gis dbang bskur bas/ de bzhin gshegs pas

52a8(rgyud): g.yas pa sha'i phyag rgya yin/ g.yon pa chang gi phyag rgya'o// mche ba g.yas dang g.yon pa yi/ bar du ma chu mnan pa ni/ g.yon pa bud med reg na

52b3(rgyud): dkyil du reg pa ni/ brda'i phyag rgyar gnas pa ste/ dbu ma'i nan tan bsgrub pa yis/ chos kyi 'khor lo chen po'i dkyil/ rang gi dbang po bsgreng ba

52b6(rgyud): ba'i phyag rgya 'di/ g.yas pa thams cad grub pa yin/ g.yon pa dbang phyug thams cad 'grub/ khu tshur g.yas dang g.yon gnyi ka/ khu tshur ba cang
52b7(rgyud): dang 'grol ba dag g.yas pargyas 'debs phyag rgya yin/ g.yon pa mi rnams thong shig pa'o// brla gnyis yongs su bsdams pa ni/ g.yas dang
52b8(rgyud): g.yon pa de bzhin te/ g.yon pa 'dod la rab tu brtson/ g.yas pa chos la brtson pa'o// dbus mo'i lha nga'i brda dag kyang // g.yas dang g.yon pa
53a1(rgyud): mnyam / @#de bzhin te/ g.yon pa 'dud pa'i phyag rgya ste// g.yas pa rab tu phyag 'tshal ba'o// dbus mo g.yas g.yon gnyis//
53a2(rgyud): dag ni/ brda yi phyag rgya rab tu gnas/ g.yas pa 'ching ba'i phyag rgya ste/ g.yon pa thams cad rnam par grol// rkang pa gnyis kyis sa mnan pa/ g.yas/
53a3(rgyud): pa g.yon pa de bzhin te/ g.yon pa thams cad gnon par byed/ g.yas pa thams cad rab tu 'joms/ dngos grub las dang bde ba dag/ 'di yis mi
53a4(rgyud): 'grub gang yang med/ rang don las rnams rab grub pa/ ma lus lus pa med par 'grub// brda'i phyag rgya shes pa'o// oM a d+hi bu zhes bya ba'i
53a5(rgyud): brda/ 'di ni phyag 'tshal zhes ston pa'o// pra ti oM a d+hi bu zhes bya ba/ phyag lan yin par shes par bya/ sems dpa' sngon dang mtha' med pa//
53a6(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba'i mchog/ sangs rgyas brda yi phyag rgya yin/ e ma'o bde ba yin par bshad/ e ma ho bde ba dpal gyi mchog/ rdo rje sems
53a7(rgyud): dpa' gang brjod pa/ sdig pa kun las thar bar 'gyur/ bde ba thams cad rab tu 'grub/ bde mchog e ma ho bde ba dang / sgrol ba de bzhin shi shi dag
53a8(rgyud): dag/ rgyas 'debs pa dang / rmongs byed dang / zab mo dag dang tshe 'bel ma/ sangs rgyas byang chub chos 'khor lo/ de bzhin khams gsum rnam par rgyal//
53b1(rgyud): 'dod pa'i lcug ma thams cad kyang / sangs rgyas brda'i phyag brgya'o// rta dang rdo rje zhal dag dang // de bzhin rdo rje snang ba dang / thal bar klog pa'i ro langs
53b2(rgyud): ma/ sangs rgyas kun gyi brda' yin no// gling bu dang ni rgyud rnams dang / de bzhin du ni rgyud gcig dang / stug po dang ni rdza rnga dag sangs rgyas brda yi phyag
53b3(rgyud): rgya'o// me tog mchod dang bdug pa mchod/ de bzhin mar me'i mchod pa dang / spos kyi mchod blo rtsi dge/ longs spong phyag brgya'i brda' yin no// de la son
53b4(rgyud): pa'i mtha' yas mchog/ chos dbyings mnyam dang mi mnyam pa// na mkha'i dbyings kyi mtha' klas pa/ lha mo kun gyi brda yin no// smin ma bskyod pa brda'
53b5(rgyud): bzhi yin/ b+ha ga ling ga e ma ho byed/ zod pa pad ma yin par bshad/ kha TaM kha yang rgyal mtshan che/ sangs rgyas phyag rgya bad mo 'dzin// bde ba kun
53b6(rgyud): gyi ra sa yan/ sangs rgyas pa yi phyag rgyar shis// shi shi sangs rgyas kun tu bshad// dkyil 'khor la ni 'khor lor bshad // de nyid dam tshig yin par
53b7(rgyud): lha rnams thams cad tshogs pas na/ skye bo dam pa kun tshogs la/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo dab pa ni/ mdza' ba thams cad 'dus pa ste/ sangs rgyas kun
53b8(rgyud): gyi brda' dag gis/ de bzhin mdza' ba 'dus par gsungs/ rdo rje sems dpa' dpal sbyor ba/ dkyil 'khor thams cad yin par bshad// lha ba
54a1(rgyud): mnyam smrathams cad kun 'dus pas/ thams cad sna tshogs bskal pa bzang / rdo rje sems dpa' dpal sbyor ba/ sangs rgyas kun tu
54a2(rgyud): kha dag sbyor bas/ rnam pa kun mkhyen shes pa'i phyir/ kun gyi slob dpon yin par bshad// kun gyi slob dpon rab gnas pa/ lha mo thams cad 'dus pas na//
54a3(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun gyi brda dag gis/ kun tu sna tshogs bskal bzang po/ de'i slob ma grub pa ni// grub pa pa yis rjes grub pa/ sangs rgyas brda ni bsang
54a4(rgyud): ba yis// rgyal tshab yin par rnam par bshad/ de las gzhan pa'i slob ma kun/ mchog dang 'bring dang tha ma rnams/ sangs rgyas kun gyi brda dag gis
54a5(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' yin par bshad/ sangs rgyas thams cad rin chen mchog/ dbu rgyan mi 'gyur dam pa ni/ sangs rgyas kun gyi rgyal srid mchog/
54a6(rgyud): yin pa rang byung rnams kyis gsungs/ thod pa'i phreng ba'i dbu rgyan dang / sangs rgyas gtsug gi nor bu dag/ sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgya yis/ dpal gyi dpal mo'o
54a7(rgyud): tshul du bshad/ sangs rgyas rang bzhin grub gcig dang / de bzhin pad mo'i rang bzhin gcig/ thams cad dbang bskur dbang bskur che/ yin par
54a8(rgyud): don grub grub pas gsungs/ yon gyi dam pa grub pa ni/ nor gyi dbyig du bshad pa ste/ snying yang nor gyi dbyig yin pas// sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgyar
54b1(rgyud): ba shad/ ga bu ra tsan dan dmar po dang / ster ba khrag chen yin par bshad/ tshogs kyi dbus su bzhag pa dpal/ thams cad ldan pa'i ra sa yan// bag ran
54b2(rgyud): las ni byas pa'i phyugs/ tsan dan dam ro po bskas pa dang / bag phyed pan las byas pa'i sha/ rgyal po zan ces gang bshad pa'o// de nas grub pa'i
54b3(rgyud): gna' bsgag pa// dam tshig ces bya bar bshad pa'o// bde mchog bde mchog ces gsungs pa/ sangs rgyas bde mchog thams cad kyis/ phyag rgya bde
54b4(rgyud): ba'i mchog tu gsungs// de bzhin e ma ho bde bai dang // snang ba zhes pa rab tu gnas// shi shi zhes pa la yang srid pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyis kyang /
54b5(rgyud): 'anga' bar bya ba ma yin pas/ sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgya yis/ phyag rgya dam tshig yin par bshad/ phyag rgyas sbyor ba yin par bshad// rdo rje sems
54b6(rgyud): dpa' dpal sbyor ba/ sbyor ba thams cad yin par bshad/ nga ni sna tshogs dam tshig ste// sa rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba che/ sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgya yis//
54b7(rgyud): sbyor ba thams cad yin par bshad/ de'i nye ba'i longs spyod ni// khams gsum thams cad ma lus pa'o// de yi gzugs dang sgra dang dri// ro dang reg pa bde mon
54b8(rgyud): ba'o// gzugs ni ri mo yin par bshad/ sgra ni glu yin zhes bshad pa'o// dri ni rab tu tshim par gsungs/ ro ni ra sa ya na yin/ reg pa bde ba yin par
55a1(rgyud): mnyam sbyibashad// rab tu reg pa dga' ba'i bde/ sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgya yis/ chos kyi sbyor ba yin par bshad/ sbyor ba'i longs spyod
55a2(rgyud): thams cad kyis// ji ltar bde ba bsten byed cing / bdag gi lhag pa'i lha sbyor ba/ rang gi mchod pa'i dam tshig yin/ rjes su sbyor bas mchod na ni/ sbyor ba kun
55a3(rgyud): gyi bde ba mchog/ sangs rgyas brda yi phyag rgya yis/ bde ba chen po yin par bshad/ ye shes bcom la snyoms 'jug pa/ rnal 'byor zhes ni bshad pa yin// sangs
55a4(rgyud): rgyas brda yi phyag rgya yis/ ting 'dzin rab tu sbyor ba 'ang bshad/ lha mo kun dang mnyam skor ba/ sangs rgyas thams cad 'dus pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor
55a5(rgyud): ba/ sangs rgyas kun gyis byin brlabs pa'o// dga' ba spyod pa grub par bshad/ rjes su sbyor ba rjes su bsgrub/ skyes pa lhar byed dga' spyod pa/ slar yang rjes su
55a6(rgyud): bsgrubs par bshad/ lha mo kun la bde sdug pa/ sbyor ba kun la mos pa ni/ kun tu sangs rgyas kun gyi bdag ra sa ya na bde bar bshad// thams cad ldang ba
55a7(rgyud): kun 'gro ba/ dngos grub dam par rab tu bshad/ dngos grub chen po ldang ba che/ sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgyar bshad// dngos grub chen po kun gyi mchog
55a8(rgyud): dbang phyug chen po bla na med/ dbang phyug kun gyi dam pa mchog/ sangs rgyas kun gyi brda yis bshad/ dngos grub chen po kun gyi mchog/ dbang phyug chen po
55b1(rgyud): bde mchog gi/ sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam spor ba/ sbyor ba'i dbang phyug bde chen ni/ khrag gi me tog yin par bshad/ mdangs ni bdug pa yin par gdag
55b2(rgyud): sha chen dag ni mar me ste/ thal ba dag na yongs su bshad/ chang ni sgeg mo yin par bshad/ rab tu myos pa sbrang rtsi'o// bu ram chang ni myos byed gsungs/
55b3(rgyud): dgun chang dag ni bdud rtsi yin/ bdud rtsi lam gyi yan lag brgyad/ sangs rgyas kun gyi brda' yin no// dgun dang sbrang rtsi gcig tu dpal/ tshwa ni 'dod chags bsra
55b4(rgyud): ba ni/ skyur po khu ba g.yon can yin/ kam pi la na bran mor bshad/ tshur ba zla ba nya ba yin/ sha ni sman gyi mchog yin no// chang ni ra sa pa nar ba shad/ zas ni
55b5(rgyud): tshe zhes bya bar bshad/ bza' ba sna tshogs grub pa ni/ sha dang chang du ldan pa dag/ dga' ba'i longs spyod bskal bzang po// tshe'i dam pa yin par bshad/
55b6(rgyud): aM mra dgun 'bum pa nas// na le ke ri a ru ka/ 'bras bu chen po khyad par dag/ bdud rtsi 'bras bu yin par bshad/ aM mra smin pa grol bar bshad/ de bzhin
55b7(rgyud): bde ba nyal ba dang // bde ba rab tu rmongs pa dag/ sangs rgyas kun gyi brda' yin no// 'bras bu chen po pa na sa/ dgun 'brum khu ba khu ba'i mchog/ na li ke
55b8(rgyud): ri dngos grub che/ dam chos 'bras bu a ru ka/ glu ni tshig tu brjod par bshad/ ngar der dag ni sil snyan yin/ sangs rgyas brda yi phyag rgya bas/ grar ni rnam
56a1(rgyud): maci sbyor/ @#/ bar rol par bshad/ rdo rje sems dpa' dpal sbyor ba'i/ glu dang sil snyan gar byed pas/ brda'i dam pas bshad par yin/ sangs rgyas kun
56a2(rgyud): gyi rnam 'phrul pa'o// rab tu zhi ba'i sil snyan glu/ gar ni shin tu rnam 'phrul ba'o// dur khrod dang ni sil snyan dang / gar ni shin tu rnam sprul pa'o// chags bcas glu dang
56a3(rgyud): sil snyan dang / gar ni shin tu rnam sprul pa'i/ mi yi dbang po sil snyan glu/ rab kyi rtsal gyis gar byas pa/ rta mchog rnam par sprul ba ni/ brda'i dam par rab tu
56a4(rgyud): bshad/ d+hi zhes bya ba mkha' gro yi/ khams gsum 'dir ni rnam par brtags/ mkha' gro ma'i phyag rgya dag mkha' gro zhes ni rab tu grags/ kun tu sna tshogs
56a5(rgyud): phyag rgya ni/ thams cad na mkhar 'gro ba ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam spor ba/ mkha' gro ma zhes rab tu grags/ sgyu ma'i gar dbang grags pa ni/ a ra
56a6(rgyud): li zhes ming du btags/ mkha' gro ma yang a ra li/ sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgya'o// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba'i/ mkha' gro ma yi dam tshig mchog/
56a7(rgyud): bcom ldan rdo rje sems dpa' dpal/ rdo rje a ra li zhes bshad pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam sbyor ba/ mkha' gro sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog/ sems dpa'
56a8(rgyud): sngon dang mtha' med pa/ rdo rje sems dpa' dga' ba'i mchog/ sangs rgyas brda'i phyag rgya yis/ di ni bskal ba bzang por bshad/ gang zhig rdo rje sems//
56b1(rgyud): dpe'i mtshan/ bskal pa bzang po zhes brjod de/ shin tu srid pa kun 'grub zhing / de ni dbang phyug chen por 'grub/ Ta ki 'dod pa yin par bshad/ dga' ba ke li ke
56b2(rgyud): la yin// byams pa chu srin yin par bshad// 'dod pa'i dbang phyug dbang dbyug mchog/ rdo rje dril bu phyag brgyad dag/ dam tshig gsum gyi dam pa yin / oM dang b+ha
56b3(rgyud): khaM kun bshad pa/ sangs rgyas brda yi phyag rgya yin/ drangs te bcug nas bcings pa dang / zhugs nas dbang du gyur pa ni/ dza hUM baM ho bshad pa ste/ sangs rgyas kun
56b4(rgyud): gyi brda' yino// a hi pa hi zhes bshad pa// tshur spyon par bzhud zhes bsgrags pa'o// ti ta ha zhes gsungs pa ni// longs la drongs shig+sa pa'o// kha kha khA hi
56b5(rgyud): zo gcig pa'o/ a ba'i zhes pa dang kyang dang / da ra da ra byin zhes pa'o/ ru ta ma kha rol cig pa'o// hu lu hu lu zhags shig pa'o// a ra ra ra bskal gcig
56b6(rgyud): pa'o// e ma'o bde ba mchog ngo mtshar ba ni/ a la la ho zhes bshad pa ni/ bde mchog rgyas 'debs phyag rgya yin/ e ma bde ba rmongs byed ma'o// snang ba
56b7(rgyud): zhes pa za ba'i rgya/ hUM shi shi na tshe 'phel ba'i// shin tu ldan dang rab tu brtan// kun tu brtan dang cher brtan pa// sangs rgyas rdo rje 'dzin pa dang // 'jig rten
56b8(rgyud): dbang dang mkha' las skyes/ shes gyur dag gyur grub par gyur// zhags nas dbang du gyur par mdzad/ oM AHa a kun bshad pa/ sangs rgyas ba rda'i
57a1(rgyud): mnyam s+hophyag rgya yin/ thabs cad mkhyen par gyur pa dang / de bzhin bde bar mkhyen pa ni/ oM sarba bid ces bshad pa ste/ sangs rgyas spyan/
57a2(rgyud): gyi phyag rgya yin/ oM ru ru bu ru dz+wa la tista sid+ha lo tsa na sarba a d+ha sadA ni/ swA hA// 'khor ba'i dngos grub mkhyen pa dang / don dam nye bar zhi ba'i phyir// sa
57a3(rgyud): rgyas rang byung bcom ldan 'das/ rnam snang mdzad ces gtso bo ni/ sangs rgyas brta'i phyag rgya yin/ bskal pa bzang po zhes bshad do// ko Ta k+Sha/ ko ta ba/
57a4(rgyud): ko Ta tsa pas sha/ ki ta rA ka/ ko la k+Sha/ ko la ba/ ko la ka sa tsa shu/ ka la b+hi sta bA/ phyag na rdo rje rang don gyi/ mtshan ma 'di rnams gang brjod pa/ de la

57a8(rgyud): gang zad dang / dgra rnams kyang ni gang bad pa// phyag na rdo rje 'dul ba'i phyir/ de ni yak+Sha yin par bshad/ he ru dpal ni ngo rje che/ bal bar 'jigs pa
57b1(rgyud): mchog yin te/ sangs rgyas kun gyi khrobo che/ brda' yis rab tu bshad pa yin/ rdo rje 'bar ba rab tu 'jig/ kha T+wAM kha dang rgyal mtshan che/ thod pa kham phor
57b2(rgyud): pad ma'i snod/ khrag chen dang ni sbrang rtsi che/ dkar mo mgu byed rab rmongs dang / ro langs ma dang lbos byed ma// gtum mo dang ni sme ma dang / lha mo bdun ni ba

58a1(rgyud): ma sbyor#nor po ma/ tri ba ba/ TaT/ tratra tra tran/ kun tu grags pa/ sangs rgyas kun gyi brda'i yin te/ dbang bskur ba dang gter dag/

59a1(rgyud): ba thor/ #ma reg rdo rje me/ ram gri me mang bdar gzhu dang / shing dang chu dang 'babacu brag/ gzugs brnyan byang ba'i khyim dag las// bya dang /

59a7(rgyud): ba'o// rdo rje sems dpa' dbas sbyor ba/ ngi k+ta'i dbyibs dang gzugs ldan pas/ rgya mtsho 'bab chu 'bab chu'i 'gram/ lha dza sa zhi ba'i chu mchog gis/

59b1(rgyud): rdo rje bdud rtsi dri ma med pa'i chu rgya mtsho zhes bya bya'i phyag rgya'o// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal sbyor ba/ ji lta'i gzugs dang dbyibs ldan pas/ mi li thod pa'i nang du
59b2(rgyud): ni/ yungs kar bskyed nas blang bar bya/ lo ma yungs kar zas su bza'// mgo bskus de bzhin 'bras bu yis/ phyogs 'tshams na mkha' sa bcings ni//
59b3(rgyud): bsrung ba kun gyi bla med pa'o// dpal don thams cad grub pa zhes bya ba'i phyag rgya'o// rdo rje sems dpa' dpal sbyor ba/ ma chu so yis legs mnan nas/ dpal
59b4(rgyud): ldan g.yon du 'gying dang bcas/ gsal bar phyogs su 'khor lo'i tshul// bla 'og drag tu byin brlabs na/ gnas gsum dag ni rgyas 'debs so// gzhug

68a1(rgyud): gyig@#rnam par mi rtog chos dgal/ rtog pa'i don 'di ji ltar gsungs/ ci slad du ni rgyang phyi ma/ dang po'i mchog 'di ji ltar lags/

68a8(rgyud): gang lags ci 'dra de bzhin te/ dkyil 'khor la ni gtso ba rnams/ rigs rnams kyi ni ji ltar lags// gsang ba dbang bskur kun de nyid/

69b3(rgyud): tham pa la/ dgu bcu dang ni ldan par bya/ zla tshes ldan la gnas pa la/ de la lnga mtho thig le yis/ spyi bo gtsug la brtag pa'o// ka dang sha de zhes pa ni/

70b1(rgyud): gnyis pa can kho na/ zla tshes gtsug dang ldan pa'i zhal/ rnam par snang mdzad rgyal chen po// kun mchog pa'i dbang phyug yin// re mig bcwo lnga brgyad
